-----title
杭州

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年</a>　娶妻徐氏。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='7141cba6760b42fb8ac1acf97b1d3275_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1109&endYear=1109')">1109年</a>　十一月己巳，进封楚国公致仕，仍提举哲宗实录。又赐以苏州南园。作品：诏赐南园示亲党。<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观末蔡京罢相欲东还诏以其园赐之京即以诗赠亲党云云。厲鶚《宋詩紀事》卷二十五 413。）</span><div id='poem_514116' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_514116' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/514116?labeling=true' target='_blank'>诏赐南园示亲党</a><span class='authorDate'>（1109年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_514116")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_514116_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_514116'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_514116'>八年帷幄竟何为<span class='inlineComment2'>（《方舆胜览》卷二作负清时）</span>，更赐南园宠退师<span class='inlineComment2'>（《吴郡志》卷一四作归）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_514116_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_514116'>堪笑当时王学士<span class='inlineComment2'>（《方舆胜览》作年王内翰）</span>，功名未有便吟诗<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_514116_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_514116'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_514116_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_514116'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_514116_0'>⑴ 宋叶梦得《石林诗话》卷下　《石林诗话》：姑苏南园，钱氏广陵王之旧圃也。王元之为长洲令，无日不携客醉饮，尝有诗曰他年我若功成后，乞取南园作醉乡。大观末，京罢相欲东还，诏以园赐之。京戏以诗示亲党云云。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_514116_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年3月1日</a>　大观庚寅季春朔，观徽宗《雪江归棹图》所题。作品：题宋徽宗雪江归棹图。<div id='poem_1198507' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198507' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198507?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题宋徽宗雪江归棹图<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观四年三月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年3月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198507")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198507_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198507'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198507'>臣伏观御制《雪江归棹图》，水远无波，天长一色，群山皎洁，行客萧条，鼓棹中流，片帆天际，雪江归棹之意尽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198507_comment'></div>天地四时之气不同，万物生天地閒，随气所运，炎凉晦明，生息荣枯，飞走蠢动，变化无方，莫之能穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198507_comment'></div>皇帝陛下以丹青妙笔，备四时之景色、究万物之情态于四图之内，盖神智与造化等也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198507_comment'></div>大观庚寅季春朔日，太师、楚国公致仕臣京谨识。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1198507_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年3月15日</a>　大观庚寅季春望，观徽宗《十八学士图》所题。作品：题宋徽宗画十八学士图。<div id='poem_1198508' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198508' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198508?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题宋徽宗画十八学士图<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观四年三月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年3月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198508")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198508_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198508'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198508'>唐太宗得杜如晦、房玄龄等十八人，佐命兴邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198508_comment'></div>臣考其施为，皆不能稽古立政；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198508_comment'></div>然终致其君至太平者，盖唐承大乱之后，饥易为食，渴易为饮，故事半古人，功已倍之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198508_comment'></div>太宗尝曰：「秦汉不足袭，三代损益如何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198508_comment'></div>房、杜不能对，遂命魏徵与玄龄等宿中书省讲议，终不能定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198508_comment'></div>太宗曰：「礼废乐坏，朕甚闵之，有志不就，古人攸悲」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198508_comment'></div>对曰：「非陛下不能行，乃臣等无素业，何愧如之」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198508_comment'></div>徵与玄龄、如晦惭慄而出，玄龄相谓曰：「有元首，无股肱，诚可叹也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198508_comment'></div>盖玄龄、如晦学非尧舜三代，其所操知秦汉，蹇浅卑近，使太宗无乡举里选、制礼作乐之功，后之学者未尝不掩卷太息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198508_comment'></div>今天下去唐又五百馀岁，皇帝陛下睿智生知，追述三代，于是乡举里选、制礼作乐，以幸天下，足以跨唐越汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198508_comment'></div>犹慨然缅想十八人，图其形，寄意于诗什，有「廱泮育贤今日盛，汇征无复隐蒿莱」之句，求贤乐士，可见于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198508_comment'></div>则成人有德，小子有造，当如圣志，十八人不足道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198508_comment'></div>大观庚寅季春望，太师、鲁国公臣京谨记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1198508_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1198508'><span class='label'>按：</span>《宋人书翰》第二集，文物出版社影印本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1198508_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年4月</a>　四月，上《哲宗实录》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年5月</a>　五月甲子，降授太子少保，依旧致仕，在外任便居住。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年1月</a>　正月，蔡京在杭州上疏反对派遣童贯出使辽国。<br /></div>
-----end

href='/Writing/1198424?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞委官编录御宝批降指挥奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰元年闰正月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1078年闰1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_1198424_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198424'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198424'>御宝批降指挥未经编录成册，恐岁月滋久，本末不全，乞委官编录。</div><div id='poem_sentence_0_1198424_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1078')">1078年8月</a>　任大理评事、权检正礼房公事。从事官制的修订。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1079&endYear=1079')">1079年8月</a>　任太子中允、馆阁校勘。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年8月</a>　为集贤校理、权提点开封府界诸县镇公事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1081&endYear=1081')">1081年</a>　在集贤校理任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年7月</a>　七月诏尚书考功员外郎蔡京编手诏，庚子，以蔡京门下省起居郎，仍同详定官制。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年7月</a>　中书御笔手诏编成。作品：中书御笔手诏编成奏。<div id='poem_1198425' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198425' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198425?labeling=true' target='_blank'>中书御笔手诏编成奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰五年七月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1082年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198425")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198425_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198425'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198425'>奉诏编中书御笔手诏，凡千三百四十六事，自治平四年抵熙宁十年，为二十一册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198425_comment'></div>乞颁付中书省。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1198425_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年2月</a>　为国子监公试撰策问试题。作品：国子监公试所策题。<div id='poem_1198503' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198503' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198503?labeling=true' target='_blank'>国子监公试所策题<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰六年二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1083年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198503")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198503_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198503'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198503'>诸司之务，寺监有所不究；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198503_comment'></div>寺监之职，六曹有所不察；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198503_comment'></div>六曹之政，都省有所不悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198503_comment'></div>任其责者，殆未足以尽小大相维、上下相制之道焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198503_comment'></div>岂制而用之者，法未足与守，推而行之者，人未足与明欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198503_comment'></div>欲度今之宜，循古之旧，而尽由其长，则事之众多，且将有迂滞之患也，诸生以为如之何则可？</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1198503_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年2月</a>　答诏问论察官。作品：答诏问论察官奏。<div id='poem_1198426' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198426' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198426?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答诏问论察官奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰六年二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1083年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198426")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198426_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198426'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198426'>窃以命官不度久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198426_comment'></div>陛下以日跻之圣，追而复之，其本末度数，皆取成于心，而断之以独智；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198426_comment'></div>故建长立属，联事合治，官无虚名，人有常守，稽古揆今，粲然备具，万世之幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198426_comment'></div>而臣猥以浅学与讨论，实自愧恨不能有益圣功之万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198426_comment'></div>窃以谓圣智作法，犹四时而成岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198426_comment'></div>自唐至周，未有一日而具者，则讲明缉熙，今日之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198426_comment'></div>而适被诏命校试诸生，故辄妄意讨论，考观诸生之政学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198426_comment'></div>言不别白，当在吏议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198426_comment'></div>陛下加惠赦臣，使毕其说，臣承命震怖，敢不尽愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198426_comment'></div>夫朝廷之有百职，百职之有佐属，犹心之运臂，臂之使指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198426_comment'></div>盖臂之作止，不期运也，而应之于心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198426_comment'></div>指之伸屈，不期使也，而应之于臂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198426_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198426_comment'></div>其血脉各相系属，而通达洞贯故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198426_comment'></div>今设官分职，有相隶之名，而未有相任之责；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198426_comment'></div>有相临之势，而未有相纠之法，此臣之所以疑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1198426_comment'></div>惟不相察，不相任，夫人得以相倚，则小吏犹豫而不敢行，大吏依违而不肯断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1198426_comment'></div>事至而莫之决，则必有受其敝者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1198426_comment'></div>苟任其责，则长贰佐属同利共忧，若手足相营也，事之不举者寡矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1198426_comment'></div>虽然，察之无时，则疲于应命，而事不加修，其说在察之以月要；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1198426_comment'></div>责之已甚，则烦于究治，而人不胜任，其说在以律下从第减。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1198426_comment'></div>如此，则士自尽而刑威矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1198426_comment'></div>或曰，今御史固察事矣，臣曰不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1198426_comment'></div>夫官府之治，有正而治之者，有旁而治之者，有统而治之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1198426_comment'></div>省曹寺监以长治属，正而治之者也，则其为法当详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1198426_comment'></div>御史非其长也，而以察为官，旁而治之者也，则其为法当略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1198426_comment'></div>都省无所不总，统而治之者也，则为法当考其成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1198426_comment'></div>然则长吏察月，御史察季，都省察岁，庶乎其可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1198426_comment'></div>臣之区区，窃意于此；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1198426_comment'></div>然以为未足以有行也，故策之于诸生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1198426_comment'></div>而诸生皆未能有至当之论，其等上者多以经义为主，至于对问之言，或取其文词而已。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1198426_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='d9af52698a65447e81b3144c8273ff2b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d9af52698a65447e81b3144c8273ff2b");'><span id='d9af52698a65447e81b3144c8273ff2b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1086')">1083-1086年</a>，37-40岁</div><div id='d9af52698a65447e81b3144c8273ff2b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年9月</a>　九月，神宗手诏分曹编修尚书省六曹条贯。每两曹差详定、检详官各一员，以便人各任责。以详定官韩忠彦、陆佃领吏、兵部，蔡京、蔡卞领户、礼部，赵彦若、王震领刑、工部。己卯，诏中书舍人蔡卞领吏、兵房，蔡京领户、刑房。王震领礼、工房，如有妨碍文字，送别房行之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年9月</a>　乞起居郎舍人隨左右分记言动。作品：乞起居郎舍人隨左右分记言动奏。<div id='poem_1198427' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198427' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198427?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞起居郎舍人随左右分记言动奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰六年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1083年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198427")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198427_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198427'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198427'>旧修起居注官二员，不分左右，每月轮一员修纂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198427_comment'></div>今起居郎、舍人分隶两省，所以备左右史官，则左当书动，右当书言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198427_comment'></div>今仍旧制，每月轮修，盖其职事未之有别，恐未足以称朝廷正名责实之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198427_comment'></div>乞自今后起居郎、舍人随左右分记言动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198427_comment'></div>如允所言，其当釐正等事即别具陈请。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1198427_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1198427'><span class='label'>按：</span>《续资治通鉴长编》卷三三九。又见同书卷三六五。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1198427_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年10月</a>　十月，起居郎蔡京、起居舍人王震并试中书舍人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年11月</a>　十一月，中书舍人蔡京为龙图阁待制，权知开封府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年</a>　三月，神宗去世。哲宗即皇帝位，太皇太后高氏垂簾听政，废除新法，打击变法派。蔡京、蔡卞兄弟一再成为被攻击和压制的对象。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年2月</a>　司马光秉政，复差役法，为期五日，同列病太迫，京独如约，悉改畿县雇役，无一违者。诣政事堂白光，光喜曰：“使人人奉法如君，何不可行之有！”<br /></div><div class='label1' id='dadcf91fc35b443780bc93c5fc537586_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("dadcf91fc35b443780bc93c5fc537586");'><span id='dadcf91fc35b443780bc93c5fc537586_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=-100000&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>，54岁</div><div id='dadcf91fc35b443780bc93c5fc537586' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年3月</a>　三月，龙图阁直学士蔡京权户部尚书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>　哲宗绍圣初由成都被召还京，盛夏过蜀道，憩遂昌官舍宝峰亭所。作品：佚诗（我行畏暑途）<span class='inlineComment2'>（姚大勇《蔡京轶诗》）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年7月</a>　乞参酌熙宁旧例讲究足国裕民之法。作品：乞参酌熙宁旧例讲究足国裕民之法奏。<div id='poem_1198428' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198428' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198428?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞参酌熙宁旧例讲究足国裕民之法奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣元年七月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198428")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198428_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198428'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198428'>神宗皇帝熙宁之初，将欲有为于天下，得王安石而任之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198428_comment'></div>于是置条例司，选天下英才，设官分职，参讲其事，兴利补弊，功烈昭著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198428_comment'></div>元祐以来，天下用度浸以匮竭，美意良法，尽遭诋诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198428_comment'></div>在于今日，正当参酌旧例，考合得宜，以称陛下追述先帝之意，以成足国裕民之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198428_comment'></div>然事之可兴者方且毛举，岂臣单力所能胜任？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198428_comment'></div>伏望圣慈检会熙宁中置条例司故事，上自朝廷大臣，下选通达世务之贤，共同考究，庶几成一代之业，以诏万世。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1198428_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年9月</a>　九月，守户部尚书。<br /><a href="javascript: showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198431?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞与张行磨勘改官奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣元年十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年12月</a>　乞依元丰条例勿闭汴河口。作品：乞依元丰条例汴河勿闭口奏。<div id='poem_1198432' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198432' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年2月</a>　请求罢合祭天地。作品：请罢合祭天地奏。<div id='poem_1198434' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198434' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198434?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请罢合祭天地奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣二年正月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1095年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198434")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198434_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198434'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198434'>先皇帝考协先王，遂罢合祭，修北郊祀地之文，更定仪注。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198434_comment'></div>遹追来孝，正在今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198434_comment'></div>而议者乃复于此尚持二三之说，谓盛夏之月不可躬祠，且当合祭，违先皇帝之诏，此臣等所未喻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198434_comment'></div>又或以谓当用孟冬纯阴之月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198434_comment'></div>神州地示，出于谶纬，郑氏祖而用之，腐儒臆决，无所经见，今奉祀大示而欲更用此礼，亦臣等所未喻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198434_comment'></div>盖地示，大祀也，而夏至之日，先王之所当行，迄魏、周、隋、唐之君，亦有能行之者，奚独至今而疑之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198434_comment'></div>请罢合祭天地，自后间，因大礼岁，以夏至之日亲祠北郊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198434_comment'></div>其亲祠北郊岁更不亲祠南郊。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1198434_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年5月</a>　建议常平免役等事专任提举官。作品：常平免役等事专任提举官奏。<div id='poem_1198435' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198435' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198435?labeling=true' target='_blank'>常平免役等事专任提举官奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣二年五月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1095年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_1198436' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198436?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请复行青苗法奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣二年七月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1095年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198436")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198436_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198436'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198436'>奉诏措置财利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198436_comment'></div>窃见熙宁中，先皇帝以天下之本在农，故稽参先王春秋补助之意，行散敛之法，薄取其息，以为放阁欠免之备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198436_comment'></div>故兼并不得专辟阖之利，而农得尽力南亩，不为兼并所困，实大惠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198436_comment'></div>行法之初，论者不一，赖先帝神武英睿，行之不疑，以克就绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198436_comment'></div>数年之后，取者云集，纳者辐至，天下仓库盈衍丰羡，而财不可胜用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198436_comment'></div>自元祐废罢以来，兼并得纵，农渐失业，向之所积，支用殆尽，以至于今，未之复也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198436_comment'></div>恭惟陛下绍述先志，将大有为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198436_comment'></div>臣愚以为生财之道，益国裕民，无以易此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198436_comment'></div>伏乞下有司检会熙宁、元丰青苗条约，参酌增损，适今之宜，立为定制，以幸天下。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1198436_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年10月</a>　卞拜右丞，以京为翰林学士兼侍读，修国史。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年4月</a>　乞募商人请香药库久卖不售之物。作品：乞募商人请香药库久卖不售之物奏。<div id='poem_1198437' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198437' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198437?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞募商人请香药库久卖不售之物奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣三年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198437")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198437_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198437'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198437'>香药库等处应出卖之物甚多，久卖不售。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198437_comment'></div>请给公据，募商人沿边入中粮草，赴户部等请。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1198437_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年5月</a>　驳孙谔论元丰元祐役法。作品：驳孙谔论元丰元祐役法奏。<div id='poem_1198438' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198438' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198438?labeling=true' target='_blank'>驳孙谔论元丰元祐役法奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣三年五月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198438")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198438_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198438'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198438'>看详谔以为元丰多，元祐省，元丰重，元祐轻，多不若省，重不若轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198438_comment'></div>则是谔以谓元丰之法不若元祐明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198438_comment'></div>而文其奸言，以为随时损益者妄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198438_comment'></div>苟以为随时损益，则元丰之法未必是，而元祐之法未必非矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198438_comment'></div>谔于陛下追绍之日敢为此言，臣切骇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198438_comment'></div>先帝谓天下土俗不同，不可概以一法，故重轻美恶，各随其宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198438_comment'></div>恐其率之不均也，故或以家业、物力，或以田亩，或以税钱，随等敷出；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198438_comment'></div>恐其久而不平也，故三年五年一造产业簿，以定高下之实，可谓均平矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198438_comment'></div>而谔于平日敢以为不均不平，其意安在？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198438_comment'></div>役钱有令五等俱出者，有自四等已上出者，有自三等以上出者，盖所用钱多，而户口偶少，则敷必至五等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198438_comment'></div>府界自熙宁、元丰只三等以上出役钱，自先帝行法之初，已不曾令五等敷出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198438_comment'></div>谔奏不以实，其意安在？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198438_comment'></div>杂职、书手有支钱，有不支者，亦各随其土俗而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198438_comment'></div>且免役法自去年五月复行，至今将一年，天下吏习而民安之，而谔以为宿弊不革者，谓熙宁、元丰之时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198438_comment'></div>以先帝有为之时为宿弊之法，则元祐之变法为革弊，而陛下今日亦不当绍而复之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198438_comment'></div>谔之意盖欲因此以疑朝廷继述之志耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1198438_comment'></div>元丰，雇法也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1198438_comment'></div>元祐，差法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1198438_comment'></div>雇与差不可并行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1198438_comment'></div>元祐固尝兼雇，已纷然无绝矣，而谔欲「无间」，是欲伸元祐之奸，惑天下之听，则昨日积斥元祐乱政之人亦当无间矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1198438_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1198438'><span class='label'>按：</span>《宋会要辑稿》食货六五之六九（第七册第六一九一页）。又见同书食货一四之九（第六册第五○四二页）。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1198438_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年5月</a>　驳孙谔论役法。作品：驳孙谔论役法奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此篇与前篇不知是否是同一奏。若不是，亦未知孰先孰后。）</span><div id='poem_1198439' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198439' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198439?labeling=true' target='_blank'>驳孙谔论役法奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣三年五月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198439")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198439_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198439'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198439'>刘挚以熙宁四年言役法十害，内第一害谓「纷错不均」，曾布以为均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198439_comment'></div>第二害，刘挚以为「贫富多少不平」，曾布以为平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198439_comment'></div>不均不平之辨已判二十年矣，谔于二十年后窃取其说，言于陛下追复之日，臣愚不知谔何心也！</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1198439_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年7月</a>　七月，蔡京为翰林学士承旨。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年9月</a>　哲宗废孟后，蔡京草废孟后诏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年12月</a>　与董敦逸辩江西役法等事。作品：与董敦逸辩江西役法等事奏。<div id='poem_1198440' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198440' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198440?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与董敦逸辩江西役法等事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣三年十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198440")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198440_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198440'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198440'>臣僚论江西役法等事，奉旨令详定重修敕令所具析闻奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198440_comment'></div>一言：「元祐初，司马光秉政，蔡京知开封府，光唱京和，首变先帝之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198440_comment'></div>只祥符一县，数日之间，差拨役人一千一百馀人，皆蔡京首为顺从」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198440_comment'></div>臣昨知开封府，于元祐元年二月内降到司马光差役法，令州县揭簿定差，其降到指挥内仍称：「如无妨碍，即便施行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198440_comment'></div>若有妨碍，限五日申奏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198440_comment'></div>其开封府虽辖诸县，自来只管勾京城内公事，应被朝旨，亦只翻录行下诸县关中而已；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198440_comment'></div>至于人户差役簿书之类，皆诸县一面施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198440_comment'></div>故当时差法，并是诸县一面定差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198440_comment'></div>其开、祥两县在辇毂之下，既见法内有「即便施行」之文，所以承行不敢少缓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198440_comment'></div>开封府虽见诸县承行之急，缘是遵依法内指挥，开封府岂敢禁止？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198440_comment'></div>然臣于是时以法令更改，上则执政大臣争论不得，下又无百姓陈诉，自非明见利害之实，未易遽夺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198440_comment'></div>亦不敢坐视更变，犹以点检骚扰催督为名，差官遍诣诸县看详商量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198440_comment'></div>又于闰二月内具状奏称：诸县申到未可施行事，乞从本府一面奏上，或因提点司看详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198440_comment'></div>寻被敕命，令与提点司同具闻奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198440_comment'></div>则臣欲具可否论列，于此可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198440_comment'></div>敕命见在，岂敢首为应和？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1198440_comment'></div>其司马光因此三次召臣到东府，诘责不差衙前，并有何利害，差官相度因依，怒见辞色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1198440_comment'></div>臣更不待所差官回，即乞外任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1198440_comment'></div>其司马光差法，开封府被受未及一月馀日，臣已罢去，遂流落外任十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1198440_comment'></div>臣之孤纵，众所共见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1198440_comment'></div>臣若能应和司马光，则必为光所知，不应变法之始，一月之间，一请遂得罢去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1198440_comment'></div>又言：「蔡京坏先帝之法，如江西吏人除重法案外，元无雇钱，近来一例创行支给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1198440_comment'></div>以百姓之脂膏，填群吏之沟壑」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1198440_comment'></div>检会江西绍圣三年敷出总数减放四万四千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1198440_comment'></div>臣若创行增添吏禄，当须于敷出总数内增过元丰额数；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1198440_comment'></div>今来比元丰有四万馀贯放免，显见臣僚妄诞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1198440_comment'></div>先帝仁政，而臣僚以为「取脂膏填沟壑」，不意敢为是言也！</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1198440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1198440'><span class='label'>按：</span>《宋会要辑稿》食货六五之七○（第七册第六一九一页）。又见同书食货一四之一一（第六册第五○四三页），《续资治通鉴长编》卷三六七原注。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1198440_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年1月</a>　哲宗下诏，黄履、蔡京、林希各举荐可充御史者一人。蔡京和林希共同推荐太学博士郑居中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年4月</a>　乞改补试外舍生月份。作品：乞改补试外舍生月份奏。<div id='poem_1198441' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198441' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198441?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞改补试外舍生月分奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣四年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198441")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198441_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198441'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198441'>三学补试外舍法，春以三月，秋以八月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198441_comment'></div>今来太学公试亦是同月，窃虑参杂。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1198441_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年8月</a>　蔡京奉旨究治“同文馆狱”<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年8月</a>　论尧舜之政。作品：论尧舜之政疏。<div id='poem_1198442' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198442' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198442?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论尧舜之政疏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣四年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198442")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198442_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198442'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198442'>文德殿视朝转对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198442_comment'></div>臣伏闻，昔者尧舜以道在天下，而以政事治之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198442_comment'></div>其道始于达四聪、明四目，而至于惇德允元、难壬人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198442_comment'></div>其政始于亲九族、平章百姓，而至于协和万邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198442_comment'></div>盖听欲聪，故达之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198442_comment'></div>视欲广，故明之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198442_comment'></div>惟聪，故无所不察，而邪说不能行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198442_comment'></div>惟明，故无所不见，而诐行不能容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198442_comment'></div>诐行不容，则能厚有德，而君子之道长；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198442_comment'></div>邪说不行，则难壬人，而小人之道消。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198442_comment'></div>故其治至于黎民于变时雍，其和至于百兽率舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198442_comment'></div>臣尝以为其道甚易知，其政甚易行，而时君世主以为高绝，莫可跂及，特未知其术耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198442_comment'></div>盖人主单立于万物之上，所以鼓舞群动，役使万物者，以能生能杀、能与能夺故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198442_comment'></div>人主操生杀与夺之柄，而以道揆天下之事，审之以仁义，济之以威权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198442_comment'></div>慢令凌政者必诛，妨功害能者必放，反覆颇僻者必窜，谗说殄行者必罚，则小大内外孰敢先后，孰敢拂违，四方将徯志而应，不劳而成矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198442_comment'></div>此皋、夔、稷、契所以吁俞，驩兜、鲧、羽所以放殛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1198442_comment'></div>其术至约而易知，非有高绝难能之行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1198442_comment'></div>臣伏睹陛下畏天爱人，有尧舜之资；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1198442_comment'></div>沈潜渊默，有尧舜之度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1198442_comment'></div>含洪光大，广览兼听，有尧舜之聪明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1198442_comment'></div>亲政四年，定志于一，而无所回夺，可谓圣矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1198442_comment'></div>操生杀与夺之柄，而坐制太平无事，万里之中国，嚬笑謦咳足以风动四方，其势未有利于此时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1198442_comment'></div>然奸党斥矣而或容，邪说察矣而未息，是非辨矣而未一，好恶审矣而未宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1198442_comment'></div>臣愚窃谓陛下退托谦抑，未以尧舜道术加天下故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1198442_comment'></div>夫生杀与夺之柄，惟人主所独制，非人臣所可共，传曰「惟名与器不可假人」是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1198442_comment'></div>陛下诚加意乎此，励劝禁于上，作威福于下，使贤者在位，而不贤者不能间，能者在职，而不才者不能夺，其以陛下之圣，尧舜不足方矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1198442_comment'></div>夫如是，则四方豪杰皆作而应陛下之求，则臣虽至愚，亦愿遂毕其说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1198442_comment'></div>臣前所谓尧舜政事者，盖《书》之称尧曰：「克明峻德，以亲九族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1198442_comment'></div>九族既睦，平章百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1198442_comment'></div>百姓昭明，协和万邦，黎民于变时雍」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1198442_comment'></div>盖治亲然后治朝廷，治朝廷然后治万民，政之序也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1198442_comment'></div>臣观今日敦宗睦族，其制法自熙宁讲定，遭元祐裁损，寖失本旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1198442_comment'></div>故服近而亲者贵极富溢，骄奢淫佚，无所不为；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1198442_comment'></div>疏而远者身为白丁，下夷编户，有饥寒之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1198442_comment'></div>且富有天下，服属虽远，皆兄弟伯叔之亲也，而或与民庶为伍，则非所以睦九族也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1198442_comment'></div>承平百年，士生斯时者众矣，三岁一举，无虑万计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1198442_comment'></div>此文王多士以宁之时，而百年休养之效也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1198442_comment'></div>员多阙少，率三岁五岁而后调一官，士皆低回苟且。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1198442_comment'></div>又无常产，因无常心，遂自溺于苟贱不廉之地，而无砥节励行之操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1198442_comment'></div>奔竞之风扇，廉耻之道衰，人材以之乏，政事以之弛，则非所谓章百姓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1198442_comment'></div>人知所尚，则士非不多也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1198442_comment'></div>土无不辟，则农非不劭也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1198442_comment'></div>器无不精，则工非不巧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1198442_comment'></div>四民之业，三民备矣，而商不通，故天下之大，百年之久，民未加富，俗未加厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1198442_comment'></div>京师者诸夏之本，诸夏者京师之末也，廛市日益消，细民日益困矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1198442_comment'></div>商农相因以为生者也，商不通则物不售，物不售则贱，贱则伤农。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1198442_comment'></div>农商不能交相养庇，四海之民，于平安之时而未免流离于水旱之际，则非所谓和万邦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1198442_comment'></div>尧舜之道，举是三者，而黎民于变时雍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1198442_comment'></div>今三者皆未得其道，此天下所以未登尧舜之盛也欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1198442_comment'></div>臣愚窃尝慨然太息，以陛下之圣，有天下之利势，而欲以登尧舜之盛，岂有难哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1198442_comment'></div>在操主柄以任贤使能，则举是三者措之天下，若反掌之易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1198442_comment'></div>夫以恩制义则九族可睦，以官任士则百姓可章，以利行商则万邦可和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1198442_comment'></div>然施之有方，行之有本，其详可得而言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1198442_comment'></div>陛下幸听，则臣愚将继今条上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1198442_comment'></div>谨先陈其大略，仰塞明诏，陛下留神加意。</div><div id='poem_sentence_54_1198442_comment'></div></div></div><br />年份未详　绍圣年间春宴时作口号。作品：绍圣春宴口号。<div id='poem_514130' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_514130' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/514130?labeling=true' target='_blank'>绍圣春宴口号<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_514130")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_514130_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_514130'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_514130'>牙牌晓奏集英班，日照云龙下九关。<div id='poem_sentence_0_514130_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_514130'>红蜡青烟寒食后，翠华黄屋太微间。<div id='poem_sentence_1_514130_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_514130'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_514130_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_514131' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_514131' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/514131?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_514131_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_514131'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_514131'>三春乐奏三春曲，万岁声连万岁山。<div id='poem_sentence_0_514131_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_514131'>欲识君臣同乐意，天威咫尺不违颜<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上宋王明清《挥麈馀话》卷一）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_514131_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_514131'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_514131_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年3月</a>　论司马光刘挚等罪状。作品：论司马光刘挚等罪状疏。<div id='poem_1198443' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198443' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198443?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论司马光刘挚等罪状奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符元年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198443")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198443_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198443'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198443'>臣等伏睹元丰八年大臣辅立陛下，内则选建亲臣以为翊赞，外则遵依法度以定纪纲，上则请垂帘权同听政以固根本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198443_comment'></div>司马光、刘挚、吕大防等忘先帝厚恩，弃君臣之义，乘时伺便，冒利无耻，交通中人张茂则、梁惟简、陈衍之徒，躐取高位，快其忿心，尽变先帝已成之法，分布党与，悉据要权，公私诋诬，无所忌惮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198443_comment'></div>既而自知其罪终不可逭，深惧一日陛下亲政，则必有欺君罔上之刑，乃回顾却虑，阴连内外，包藏祸心，密为倾摇之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198443_comment'></div>于是疏隔两宫，及随龙内侍十人悉行放罢，以去陛下之腹心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198443_comment'></div>废受遗顾命元臣，置以必死之地，先帝任事之人无一存者，以剪陛下之羽翼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198443_comment'></div>先帝之所治而得罪者纵而释之，以立陛下之仇敌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198443_comment'></div>先帝之所恶而弃者收而用之，以植陛下之怨雠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198443_comment'></div>以王府为要途，以朝廷归私室，上下协比，同恶相济，意在不测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198443_comment'></div>天锡陛下圣知，沉机渊默，不言九年，侧身端拱，无毫釐之差，群奸无以伺其隙，众恶不能成其志，宗庙之灵，社稷之福也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198443_comment'></div>此固不待指数，而天下晓然易知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198443_comment'></div>然奸党交结，其操心危，虑患深，踪迹诡秘，世莫得闻，至于焚弃毁灭，无复考验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198443_comment'></div>前日虽已窜逐摈废，而奸谋逆节盖未白于天下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198443_comment'></div>臣等幸被诏旨询究本末，乃于焚弃毁灭之馀，得其情状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198443_comment'></div>其无君之恶，同司马昭之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198443_comment'></div>擅事之迹，过赵高指鹿之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198443_comment'></div>天地之所不容，人神之所共弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1198443_comment'></div>盖至今日，其恶遂彰明较著如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1198443_comment'></div>臣等窃睹上项事节大逆不道，迹状明白，揆之以义，谳之以法，死有馀责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1198443_comment'></div>所有臣衍罪在不赦，亦乞更赐审问，正以国法。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1198443_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年3月</a>　定验咸阳民段义所献玉玺。作品：定验咸阳民段义所献玉玺奏。<div id='poem_1198444' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198444' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198444?labeling=true' target='_blank'>定验咸阳民所献玉玺奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符元年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198444")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198444_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198444'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198444'>奉敕讲议定验咸阳民段义所献玉玺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198444_comment'></div>臣等取责段义状，委于绍圣三年十二月内河南乡刘银村修造家舍掘土得之，即不是茔域内收到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198444_comment'></div>曾有光照满室，及篆文官称，篆文与秦相李斯篆文合，有鱼龙凤鸟之形，是古之虫篆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198444_comment'></div>考其体法，自汉唐而下金石遗文，笔法精妍无若此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198444_comment'></div>又玉工言，玉玺制作即非今来工匠可造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198444_comment'></div>臣等取到秘阁所收《玉玺谱》记录，与历代史书参照，皆不相合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198444_comment'></div>今止以历代正史所载为据，略去诸家与传注之缪，考验传授之实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198444_comment'></div>案所献玉玺，其色绿如蓝，温润而泽，其文曰「受命于天，既寿永昌」，背螭纽间有小窍，用以贯组。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198444_comment'></div>又得玉螭首一，其玉白如膏，亦温润；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198444_comment'></div>其背亦螭纽五盘，纽间亦有贯纽小窍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198444_comment'></div>其面无文，与玺相合，大小方阔，无毫发差殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198444_comment'></div>篆文工作，皆非近世所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198444_comment'></div>臣等今考，玺之文曰「皇帝寿昌」者，晋玺也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198444_comment'></div>曰「受命于天」者，后魏玺也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198444_comment'></div>「有德者昌」者，唐玺也，「惟德允昌」者，石晋玺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198444_comment'></div>则「既寿永昌」者，秦玺可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1198444_comment'></div>今得玺于咸阳，其玉乃蓝田之色，其篆乃李斯小篆体，其文则刻而非隐起，其字则饰以龙凤鸟鱼，乃虫书鸟迹之法，其制作尚象古而不华，于今所传古书莫可比拟，而工作篆文之巧者亦莫能髣髴，非汉以后所能作亦明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1198444_comment'></div>今陛下仰承天休，嗣守祖宗大宝，而神玺自出，其文曰「受命于天，既寿永昌」，则天之所畀，乌可忽哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1198444_comment'></div>古之王天下者，其盛莫如周，惟赤刀、宏璧、琬琰大玉、天球、河图、舞衣、兑之戈、和之弓、垂之矢，以为重宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1198444_comment'></div>汉、晋以来，得宝鼎瑞物，犹告庙改元，肆眚上寿，况传国之器乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1198444_comment'></div>或曰：秦所作，何足宝哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1198444_comment'></div>然汉高祖破秦而得之，光武降盆子而受之，主为服用，号曰传国，而祠高庙，赐民爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1198444_comment'></div>若东晋渡江，世以无玺为讥，乃或设谲诈兴师以取之，盖其重如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1198444_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下事天之诚，事地之孝，明察著见，而盛德日跻，将以合天地之化，故灵符效祉，神宝出应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1198444_comment'></div>其所以昭受命，非竭诚尽礼，不足以称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1198444_comment'></div>臣等被奉诏旨，得与讨论，黜诸家伪说，而断以正史，考验甚明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1198444_comment'></div>所有玉玺委是汉以前传国之宝，法物礼仪，乞所属施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1198444_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年4月</a>　乞废弃刘挚诸子罚其同党。作品：乞废弃刘挚诸子罚其同党奏。<div id='poem_1198445' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198445' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198445?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞废弃刘挚诸子罚其同党奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符元年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198445")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198445_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198445'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198445'>臣昨奉诏究问文及甫书事，寻具进呈，乞赐施行，至今未奉朝旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198445_comment'></div>伏缘刘挚与其同罪，有司马昭之心，为同时之人所发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198445_comment'></div>而陛下以天地之度，贷其万死，恩至厚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198445_comment'></div>而臣拳拳犹有请者，欲正其典刑，以及其子孙，以信于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198445_comment'></div>今挚已物故，子孙虽有广南居住指挥，而未闻有废弃之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198445_comment'></div>至于同恶之人，前物故与未物故者俱未有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198445_comment'></div>且人臣有司马昭之心，大逆无以加，此则凡知事君者莫不切齿，而旷日引久，未闻行遣，此臣之所未喻者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198445_comment'></div>夫罚罪，陛下之威柄，今大逆不道之罪，而得逃于今日，臣愚以为非所以示天下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198445_comment'></div>伏望早降指挥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1198445_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年6月</a>　翰林学士承旨蔡京等上《常平、免役勅令格式》，将常平（即青苗）、免役、农田水利、保甲等法总为一书，颁之天下。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年7月</a>　乞惩治刘挚党附显著之人。作品：乞惩治刘挚党附显著之人第三奏。<div id='poem_1198446' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198446' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198446?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞惩治刘挚党附显著之人第三奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符元年七月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198446")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198446_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198446'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198446'>臣昨论奏文及甫所发刘挚有司马昭之心，及其党附之人，废其子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198446_comment'></div>伏闻刘挚、梁焘已有处分，其馀显著之人未有指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198446_comment'></div>且挚等逆心，及甫言之于元祐挚、焘用事之时，则其事可信不诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198446_comment'></div>在法，九族当坐，今陛下许其不死，贷其九族，父母之恩，天地之造也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198446_comment'></div>臣闻陛下好生克己，盛德敢不奉承，然至于罪均罚殊，不足以称，则臣之拳拳，与有职责，岂敢自已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198446_comment'></div>且挚之逆心，及甫以为行道之人皆知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198446_comment'></div>行道之人不归之他人，而归之挚等，盖其心非隐晦深秘不可晓者，固不待究穷推原，自已彰明较著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198446_comment'></div>则其一时党附显著之人，同恶相济，岂得无为之议者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198446_comment'></div>或曰：使有是心，特出于及甫雠忿之言，无可考信，难正其罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198446_comment'></div>臣愚窃以为过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198446_comment'></div>臣请以朋党之人论之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198446_comment'></div>刘安世尝论禁中雇乳母为陛下已亲女宠，又论不御经筵，谓陛下已惑酒色，诬罔圣躬为甚也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198446_comment'></div>方奸臣擅事，以无为有，形于章疏者果何心哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198446_comment'></div>其心迹可验于此，而谓之无可考信者，不知其说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198446_comment'></div>使其事不彰露则已，今差官究问，事状暴著，天下之愤疾不平，以为朝奏其罪，夕正其法矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198446_comment'></div>初则三省受告言而不施行，匿明氏进状而不奏禀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1198446_comment'></div>今又旷日引久，几年于此，举其一而违其众，流俗因得藉其口，天下亦遂疑其罪，臣又不知其说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1198446_comment'></div>刘挚生则身被远斥，死则废及子孙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1198446_comment'></div>而岩叟生不及其身，死不及其子，安世又不问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1198446_comment'></div>罪罚殊科如此，臣又不知其说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1198446_comment'></div>借使及甫与挚有雠，其言出于忿心，然及甫乃元祐奸党，闻其父言，具知其事，使无忿心，何从而发大逆不道？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1198446_comment'></div>在律，六亲皆得告言，况雠人与有忿心者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1198446_comment'></div>恭惟陛下天纵圣德，自初嗣服，不言九年，所以臣奸无所乘间，元恶不能措手，言之可为寒心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1198446_comment'></div>幸而为及甫忿心所发，又幸而元祐五年与邢恕书尚在，故奸心无所逃遁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1198446_comment'></div>而乃持其事，缓其罚者何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1198446_comment'></div>岂在位者挚党多欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1198446_comment'></div>为挚说者亦多欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1198446_comment'></div>伏望陛下奋以独断，明君臣之义，正国家之刑，检会臣等奏，布告天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1198446_comment'></div>及检会王岩叟、刘安世所奏章疏，考验心迹，并依挚、焘例施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1198446_comment'></div>更有显著之人如安世者，亦乞检会，一起行遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1198446_comment'></div>所有受明氏告言刘挚大逆进状，其不曾进呈官司，亦乞以其事下刑部、大理寺约法，以正典刑，永为惩戒，所以解天下之惑。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1198446_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年4月</a>　乞续修《华戎信录》作品：乞续修华戎信录奏。<div id='poem_1198447' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198447' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198447?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞续修华戎信录奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符二年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198447")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198447_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198447'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198447'>窃实修《华戎信录》，自通好以来，事无不载，粲然可观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198447_comment'></div>而所载止于元丰六年，后来未经编录，伏望委官续成。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1198447_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年6月</a>　乞许翰林学士先次挑班上殿。作品：乞许翰林学士先次挑班上殿奏。<div id='poem_1198448' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198448' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198448?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞许翰林学士先次挑班上殿奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符二年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198448")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198448_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198448'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198448'>臣等每缘职事请对，待次或踰旬日，方得瞻望清光；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198448_comment'></div>而文字遇有急速，深恐失事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198448_comment'></div>伏望指挥下閤门，今后许翰林学士依六曹、开封府例，先次挑班上殿，仍不隔班。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1198448_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年1月</a>　正月哲宗崩，徽宗继位，向太后权同听政。翰林学士承旨蔡京受命起草哲宗遗制。作品：哲宗遺制。<div id='poem_1198417' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198417' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198417?labeling=true' target='_blank'>哲宗遗制</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符三年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198417")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198417_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198417'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198417'>朕嗣守大业，十有六年，永惟付托之重，夙夜祗惧，靡敢遑宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198417_comment'></div>赖天之休，方内乂安，蛮夷率服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198417_comment'></div>乃自故冬以来，数冒大寒，浸以成疾，药石弗效，遂至弥留，恐不获嗣言，以诏列位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198417_comment'></div>皇弟端王某，先帝之子，而朕之爱弟也，仁孝恭俭，闻于天下，宜授神器，以昭前人之光，可于柩前即皇帝位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198417_comment'></div>皇太后、皇太妃保佑朕躬，恩德至厚，凡在礼数，其议所以增崇，以称朕欲报无已之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198417_comment'></div>方嗣君践祚之初，应军国事，请皇太后权同处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198417_comment'></div>应诸军赏给，并取嗣君处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198417_comment'></div>丧服以日易月，山陵制度，务从俭约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198417_comment'></div>在外群臣止于本处举哀，不得擅离治所，成服三日而除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198417_comment'></div>应缘边州镇皆以金革从事，不用举哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198417_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198417_comment'></div>死生之期，理有必至，宗社之奉，其永无疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198417_comment'></div>尚赖股肱近臣，中外百辟，协辅王室，底绥万邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198417_comment'></div>咨尔臣民，咸体朕意。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1198417_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年3月</a>　三月，朝廷原定翰林学士承旨蔡京以端明殿学士兼龙图阁学士出知太原府，随之受到向太后强烈反对，蔡京依前复翰林学士承旨，留修神宗史。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年4月</a>　哲宗皇帝謚議。<div id='poem_1198449' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198449' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198449?labeling=true' target='_blank'>哲宗皇帝谥议</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符三年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198449")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198449_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198449'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198449'>臣闻道有常道，名有常名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198449_comment'></div>道无乎不在，而名未始有极，此道与名之常也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198449_comment'></div>古之圣人得道之常，以入于有，即其应物之迹，而名随焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198449_comment'></div>虽所称异号，而道之所谓常名者固存乎其中矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198449_comment'></div>恭惟大行皇帝以天纵之圣，承百年积累之业，越在冲幼，履帝之位，若固有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198449_comment'></div>体道以为德，故寂然不动，有以见天下之赜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198449_comment'></div>明而用晦，盖不言者九年，及南面而听天下，疏观万物，泛应曲当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198449_comment'></div>其辟也开而天，而阖也渊而神，虽左右之人莫能察其喜怒之色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198449_comment'></div>临下以简，制动以静，可谓盛德之至，无得而名言者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198449_comment'></div>然臣考之前载，质诸先王，柔外直内谓之钦，经天纬地谓之文，思以作圣谓之睿，戡定暴乱谓之武，无小不见谓之昭，继志述事谓之孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198449_comment'></div>于是窃迹盛德大业，著于事为而可以形容者，条列而拟象之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198449_comment'></div>盖外温恭而内允塞，钦天之威，遇灾而惧，顺帝之则，小心翼翼，动容周旋，必中于礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198449_comment'></div>望之如天之不可度，就之如日之温而可爱，可谓钦矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198449_comment'></div>沉潜刚克，高明柔克，刚柔错综，以济其用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198449_comment'></div>尊钦儒学，以缉熙于光明，罢黜章句之小道，发明六艺之科指，可谓文矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198449_comment'></div>致虚以为明，致一以为思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1198449_comment'></div>思而后言，言简而切；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1198449_comment'></div>迫而后动，动而不跲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1198449_comment'></div>扩而充之，至于大而能化之圣，可谓睿矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1198449_comment'></div>不令而威，不严而肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1198449_comment'></div>偏师裨将，授以成算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1198449_comment'></div>乘边出塞，不顿一戟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1198449_comment'></div>开疆辟地，列阵置守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1198449_comment'></div>羌人扶杖而请罪，陇右稽颡而乞降，可谓武矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1198449_comment'></div>吉之先见，独观乎昭旷之原，衡听万事而不惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1198449_comment'></div>于是非取舍之际，富善人，敦有德，或自一言而知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1198449_comment'></div>难任人，堲谗说，或由一见而察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1198449_comment'></div>光被四表，不遗微小，可谓昭矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1198449_comment'></div>遹骏其声，丕承其烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1198449_comment'></div>悼法度之扫荡，则当宁太息；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1198449_comment'></div>愤奸罔之诬訾，则敛容出涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1198449_comment'></div>政无小大，追而复之，不夺于浮言，不移于异意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1198449_comment'></div>熙宁、元丰之政，得复行于今日，可谓孝矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1198449_comment'></div>故十有六年，海内乂安，百姓蒙福，天地协应，奸宄不作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1198449_comment'></div>神宝自至，祥光属天，时和岁丰，物无疵疠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1198449_comment'></div>遐荒幽远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1198449_comment'></div>毡裘毳服左衽之俗，莫不面内而来臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1198449_comment'></div>方慨然欲有为，以追迹三代之隆，志未就而上宾，此万国所以摧心，三灵为之变色也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1198449_comment'></div>虽殚天下之美，固不足以名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1198449_comment'></div>而百辟卿士，齐心涤虑，合天下之公，即南郊之阳，以请命于上帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1198449_comment'></div>乃按谥法曰：威仪悉备曰钦，道德博闻曰文，象方盖平曰睿，阐境斥土曰武，圣钦日跻曰昭，继志成事曰孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1198449_comment'></div>合是众德，以为之名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1198449_comment'></div>垂是后世，于是为称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1198449_comment'></div>然古之王天下者，考祖有功而宗有德，德之可宗者莫大乎哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1198449_comment'></div>昔之称尧曰「知人则哲，惟帝其难之」，称舜曰「浚哲文明」，称成汤至于帝乙曰「经德秉哲」，称太王至武王曰「世有哲王」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1198449_comment'></div>窃考大行皇帝运量酬酢，万世所得而宗者哲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1198449_comment'></div>盖帝之所难，而王之所繇兴，非天下之至明，其孰能与于此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1198449_comment'></div>大行皇帝宜天锡之曰钦文睿武昭孝皇帝，庙号哲宗。</div><div id='poem_sentence_47_1198449_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年5月10日</a>　徽宗召见口谕京草草复孟后位制。作品：親奉聖語札子。<div id='poem_1198451' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198451' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198451?labeling=true' target='_blank'>亲奉圣语劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年5月10日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198451")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198451_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198451'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198451'>元符三年五月十日，召赴内东门小殿，上曰：「废后久处瑶华，皇太后极所矜怜，今欲复其位号，召卿草制」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198451_comment'></div>奏曰：「臣曾草废后诏，今又草复后制，臣岂得无罪」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198451_comment'></div>上曰：「此岂干卿事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198451_comment'></div>兼皇太后言，昨先帝既废后，亦有悔意，曾语与皇太后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198451_comment'></div>今先帝上仙，追前意与复位号，于理无嫌」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198451_comment'></div>臣京对曰：「古无两后，今日因皇太后恩怜，理亦无妨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198451_comment'></div>但臣闻有复必有废，未知圣意如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198451_comment'></div>存之何害？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198451_comment'></div>废之何益」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198451_comment'></div>上曰：「元符皇后先帝所立，位号已定，岂可更废之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198451_comment'></div>适足以彰先帝之失」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198451_comment'></div>臣京曰：「圣意如此，天下幸甚」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198451_comment'></div>元符皇后存之何害于朝廷？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198451_comment'></div>废之适足快报怨于先帝之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198451_comment'></div>存废于朝廷无利害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198451_comment'></div>恭闻德音，有以见陛下尽兄弟之义，皇太后敦母爱之仁，天下幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1198451_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1198451'><span class='label'>按：</span>《鸡肋编》卷中，中华书局一九八三年校点本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1198451_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年5月</a>　五月，向太后主张恢复孟氏的哲宗皇后位，徽宗命蔡京草复孟后位制。作品：復元祐皇后制。<div id='poem_1198418' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198418' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198418?labeling=true' target='_blank'>复元祐皇后制</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符三年五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198418")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198418_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198418'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198418'>门下：朕绍休列圣，承训东朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198418_comment'></div>施惠行仁，既诞孚于有众；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198418_comment'></div>念今追往，用敦叙于我家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198418_comment'></div>废后孟氏，顷自勋门，嫔于王室，得罪先帝，退处道宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198418_comment'></div>逮兹累年，克庸祗德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198418_comment'></div>皇太后念仙游之寖邈，抚前事以兴悲，恻然深矜，示不终废，申崇位叙，还复宫庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198418_comment'></div>乃诏辅臣，具依审议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198418_comment'></div>虽元符建号，已正位于中宫，而永泰上宾，固无嫌于并后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198418_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198418_comment'></div>源情起义，盖示亲亲之恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198418_comment'></div>克己慎身，宜成妇妇之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198418_comment'></div>其率循于懿范，以上答于深仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198418_comment'></div>往服茂恩，永膺多福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198418_comment'></div>可复为元祐皇后。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1198418_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年5月</a>　议太庙迁祔。作品：太庙迁祔议。<div id='poem_1198450' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198450' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198450?labeling=true' target='_blank'>太庙迁祔议</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符三年五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198450")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198450_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198450'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198450'>窃考《书》称：「七世之庙，可以观德」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198450_comment'></div>《礼·王制》曰：「三昭三穆，与太祖之庙而七」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198450_comment'></div>则七庙之制，自先王以来，于今未之有改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198450_comment'></div>恭惟哲宗皇帝嗣神宗皇帝大统，父子相承，自当为世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198450_comment'></div>今若不祧远祖，不以哲宗为世，则是三昭四穆与太祖之庙而八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198450_comment'></div>谓宜深考礼经，迁祔如礼。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1198450_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年12月</a>　修成《太学敕令式》二十三册。作品：修成太学敕令式奏。<div id='poem_1198452' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198452' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198452?labeling=true' target='_blank'>修成太学敕令式奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符三年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198452")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198452_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198452'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198452'>奉敕详定国子监三学并外州军学制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198452_comment'></div>今修成《太学敕令式》二十三册，以「绍圣新修」为名。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1198452_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年8月</a>　元符三年八月八日哲宗皇帝第四女杨国公主葬于河南府永安县。作品：宋杨国公主墓志铭。<div id='poem_1198520' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198520' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198520?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋杨国公主墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符三年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198520")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198520_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198520'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198520'>杨国公主，哲宗皇帝第四女，母曰皇后刘氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198520_comment'></div>绍圣四年九月十八日生于宫閤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198520_comment'></div>生踰年，锁学士院，宣制文德殿下，封为懿宁公主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198520_comment'></div>年三岁，元符二年闰九月二十八日夜，暴得惊疾，趣国医胗视，医云：「主疾已革」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198520_comment'></div>越翌日薨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198520_comment'></div>哲宗震悼，辍视朝三日，赠魏国公主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198520_comment'></div>皇后率从卫护主出内，命宣庆使、明州观察使、入内内侍侍省押班冯世宁管句，权厝于奉先资福禅院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198520_comment'></div>公主姿容，性聪慧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198520_comment'></div>既晬，见玩好之具，皆默识之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198520_comment'></div>今上即位，追封杨国公主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198520_comment'></div>以三年七月二十日起菆，诏有司具一品卤簿，遣使以少牢、香币、赠玉、黠纁告祭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198520_comment'></div>是年八月八日葬于河南府永安县永泰之侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198520_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1198520'>有美懿宁，惟帝季女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198520_comment'></div>疾不及医，胡夺之遽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198520_comment'></div>庑庑陵原，万世之固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198520_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1198520'>翰林书艺局玉册官臣□惠迪刻<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1198520_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1198520'>题后原署：「翰林学士承旨、中大夫、知制诰、兼侍读、修国史、上柱国、南阳郡开国公<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>、食邑二千三百户、<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>食实封二百户、赐紫金鱼袋臣蔡京撰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1198520_comment'></div>翰林书艺局艺学、兼讲筵应奉御书臣李安中书并篆盖」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1198520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1198520'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_15_1198520_0'>⑴ 民国《巩县志》卷一七，民国二十六年泾川图书馆刻本。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_16_1198520_8'>⑵ 按：「开国公」原作「开封」，据后《尹国公妻刘氏墓志铭》改</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_16_1198520_9'>⑶ 按：《尹国公妻刘氏墓志铭》作「三百户」</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1198520_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年8月</a>　元符三年八月八日宗室赵士䛲葬于河南府永安县。作品：宋宗室右班殿直墓記。<div id='poem_1198521' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198521' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198521?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋宗室右班殿直墓记</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符三年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198521")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198521_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198521'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198521'>君讳士谩，字信之，故平阳懿恭王允升之曾孙，东阳安宪王宗悌之孙，感德军节度观察留后仲顗之幼子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198521_comment'></div>所生母杨氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198521_comment'></div>君生而俊秀，稍长，知事父兄以孝顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198521_comment'></div>洎出就学，宾礼师友，祗敬肃庄，同小家窭人子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198521_comment'></div>屈首授经，不烦教勒，日记数百言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198521_comment'></div>执笔临书，一学即可观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198521_comment'></div>閒赋诗，数数有可喜语，识者赏其不凡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198521_comment'></div>年五岁赐名，授右班殿直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198521_comment'></div>十岁，以《孝经》、《论语》试诵学官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198521_comment'></div>十有五岁，得疾，七日卒，实元符三年三月十二日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198521_comment'></div>族党莫不悲恸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198521_comment'></div>以是年八月八日，祔葬于河南府永安县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198521_comment'></div>谨记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198521_comment'></div>翰林承旨、知制诰、侍读、修国史、柱国、南阳郡开国信邑蔡京撰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198521_comment'></div>御书官李安中书<span class='inlineComment2'>（民国《巩县志》卷一七。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198521_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1198521'>南阳郡开国信邑：疑有误，后《尹国公妻刘氏墓志铭》作「南阳郡开国公食邑三百户……」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1198521_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年8月</a>　元符三年八月八日宗室感德军节度使尹国公妻普宁郡君刘氏葬于河南府永安县。作品：宋宗室感德军节度使尹国公妻普宁郡君刘氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1198522' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198522' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198522?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋宗室感德军节度使尹国公妻普宁郡君刘氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符三年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198522")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198522_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198522'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198522'>感德军节度使、尹国公令谷夫人、普宁郡君刘氏，曾祖谦，保静军节度使、殿前都指挥使、赠中书令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198522_comment'></div>祖□选，左迁库副使、赠左迁牛卫上将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198522_comment'></div>□□□，故东头供奉官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198522_comment'></div>母长兴县□赵氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198522_comment'></div>庆历三年九月生于祖第，幼岐□□□不为□戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198522_comment'></div>至和二年，归尹国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198522_comment'></div>入谢禁中，恩赐以冠帔，仍封长乐县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198522_comment'></div>夫人以事父者事其舅南康脩孝王，以事母者事其姑南康郡太夫人，孝□隆□□宗党称焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198522_comment'></div>治平四年，南康感疾，夫人亲调汤剂，至刺血为疗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198522_comment'></div>明年，脩孝不豫，如事南康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198522_comment'></div>及持丧，哀毁瘵瘠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198522_comment'></div>元祐元年，尹国公迁贵州防□使，追封普宁郡君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198522_comment'></div>四年薨，夫人以伉俪之义，哀悲昼夜不息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198522_comment'></div>既葬，杜门绝往来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198522_comment'></div>治家严肃，以经术教其子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198522_comment'></div>绍圣三年，男子照以本经第□□□，夫人喜曰：「不违尔父之志矣，吾无憾焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1198522_comment'></div>性温厚，御群妾，加以慈，□及娣姒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1198522_comment'></div>衣服浣濯，食不重味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1198522_comment'></div>尤无妒忌□行，喜愠不形于颜色，虽老□□□□□□居□二年，中外肃然，可谓贤矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1198522_comment'></div>元符三年五月十三日，疾终于正寝，享年五十有九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1198522_comment'></div>子男四人：长子柳，方赐名而亡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1198522_comment'></div>次子昭，右监门卫大将军，□十三日而卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1198522_comment'></div>二人幼亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1198522_comment'></div>女三人：长适内殿崇班李仔，次适内殿崇班杨公谅，三人早夭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1198522_comment'></div>孙男四人：长伯端，三班□□，□未名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1198522_comment'></div>孙女三人：长适□□□□□，其馀并幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1198522_comment'></div>以其年八月八日祔葬于河南府永安县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1198522_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1198522'>□宗之甥，笃敬□爱，岐嶷夙成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1198522_comment'></div>□事其姑，丧致其哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1198522_comment'></div>克己弗渝，行弗□□。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1198522_comment'></div>凡厥后人，斯言可□。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1198522_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_1198522'>□□□玉册官臣□□刻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1198522_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='643e0dc29a604319a367841f41b055a9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("643e0dc29a604319a367841f41b055a9");'><span id='643e0dc29a604319a367841f41b055a9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=-100000&endYear=1109')">1109年</a>，63岁</div><div id='643e0dc29a604319a367841f41b055a9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年5月</a>　韩忠彦与曾布交恶，谋引京自助，复用为学士承旨。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年7月</a>　忠彦罢，拜尚书左丞，俄代曾布为右仆射。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年8月</a>　徽宗命相之后即诏置讲议司，命蔡京提举。作品：举讲议司僚属奏。<div id='poem_1198453' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198453' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198453?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举讲议司僚属奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁元年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198453")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198453_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198453'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198453'>奉手诏提举讲议司，仍令遴拣乃僚，共议因革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198453_comment'></div>伏见户部尚书吴居厚、翰林学士张商英、刑部侍郎刘赓，才猷敏邵，练达世务，欲乞差充详定官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198453_comment'></div>起居舍人范致虚、太常少卿王汉之、仓部郎中黎珣、吏部员外郎叶棣乞差充参详官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198453_comment'></div>臣伏读手诏，如宗室、冗官、国用、商旅、盐泽、赋调及尹牧事，皆政之大者，臣欲每事委官三员讨论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198453_comment'></div>并乞差充检讨文字，有见任者令兼领，不可兼及在外者并权罢见任，赴司供职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198453_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1198453'>熙宁条例司检详文字、编修及编定并在司分遣出外，相度共一十九人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198453_comment'></div>今事有多寡，人力有馀或不足，乞从本司随事分委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198453_comment'></div>仍乞以承奉郎乔方、鄂州司户参军沈锡充尹牧检讨官。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1198453_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年8月22日</a>　蔡京奏请“以学校为今日先务，乞天下并置学养士。”作品：乞天下置学养士奏。<div id='poem_1198454' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198454' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198454?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞天下置学养士奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁元年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年8月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198454")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198454_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198454'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198454'>乞罢开封府解额，除量留五十人充开封府土著人取应外，馀并改充天下贡士之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198454_comment'></div>诸州军额各取三分之一添充贡士额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198454_comment'></div>乞天下并置学养士，郡小或应举人少，则令三二州学者聚学于一州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198454_comment'></div>置州学，并差教授，先置一员，在学生员及百人已上，申乞添置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198454_comment'></div>不拘资序，并许选差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198454_comment'></div>应元祐以来教授条制更不施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198454_comment'></div>应本路常平户绝田土物业，契勘养士合用数拨充；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198454_comment'></div>如不足，以诸色系官田宅物业补足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198454_comment'></div>请以太学三舍校试法删立颁降，升补为上舍生者听每二年贡入太学，随太学上舍试，仍别为号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198454_comment'></div>若试中上等，补充太学上舍中等；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198454_comment'></div>试中中等者，补充下等；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198454_comment'></div>试中下等者，补内舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198454_comment'></div>馀为外舍生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198454_comment'></div>虽不入等，及科举遗逸，而学行为乡里所服，委知州、通判、监司依贡士法贡入；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198454_comment'></div>委祭酒、司业、博士询考得实，当议量材录用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198454_comment'></div>每路自朝廷选监司二人提举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1198454_comment'></div>知通令佐仍每十日一诣学，监司一岁巡遍所部州学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1198454_comment'></div>凡贡士，自教授考选推择，申州；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1198454_comment'></div>知州、通判审察，监司覆按，监司、知州、通判连书闻奏，随奏遣赴太学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1198454_comment'></div>若所贡非其人，或应举而不贡，一等依律科罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1198454_comment'></div>若贡士到太学试中上等，及考选升舍人多，即等第立法推赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1198454_comment'></div>请天下诸县皆置学，令佐掌之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1198454_comment'></div>学置长、谕各一人，并支俸禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1198454_comment'></div>并职事人，相度随宜量置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1198454_comment'></div>除倚郭县不置外，有不置教授处，其州学听置，仍只依县学法，以知州、通判主之，及于本县委令佐擘画地利，及不系省杂收钱内桩充费用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1198454_comment'></div>诸学生在县学一年，学长、学谕考选行艺，报令佐审实，申州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1198454_comment'></div>知、通验实，教授试其文艺，以入州学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1198454_comment'></div>不置教授州依此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1198454_comment'></div>应州县学生，若外舍在学实及二年，五犯规矩，两犯第三等已上罚，并五试不中第三等，而文艺无可取之实，行能无可教之资，立出学之法，则在学者不敢不勉，在外者有阙可试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1198454_comment'></div>既屏之出学，却许入县学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1198454_comment'></div>又三犯规矩，犯第三等已上罚，并五试不中第三等，则屏之出学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1198454_comment'></div>若犯杖已上罪，终身不齿，永不得入州县学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1198454_comment'></div>历在外官子弟亲戚，法不合在本处取应者，许随处入学，即不得升补与贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1198454_comment'></div>在学通及一年，不犯第二等已上罚，给公据，许赴太学取应，国子监解名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1198454_comment'></div>知州、通判、教授选补职事不当，并依贡士法降二等坐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1198454_comment'></div>请除见行书史外，应邪说异书悉不许教授。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1198454_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1198454'><span class='label'>按：</span>《宋会要辑稿》崇儒二之七。第三册第二一九○页又见《通鉴长编纪事本末》卷一二六，《群书考索》后集卷二八，《文献通考》卷四六，《宋史》卷一五七《选举志》三。《宋会要辑稿》崇儒二之九（第三册第二一九一页）。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1198454_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年10月</a>　置外学，赐名辟雍，上舍三百人，内舍六百人，外舍三千人。作品：外学条件奏。<div id='poem_1198455' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198455' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198455?labeling=true' target='_blank'>外学条件奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁元年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198455")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198455_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198455'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198455'>窃以周制，大司乐掌成均之法，以治建国之学政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198455_comment'></div>而王国之外，则党有庠，遂有序，卿大夫由是以兴贤能焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198455_comment'></div>故《王制》述四代之学，亦曰：「周人养国老于东胶，养庶老于虞庠」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198455_comment'></div>虞庠在国之西郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198455_comment'></div>先儒谓四代之学，或上西，或上东，或贵在国，或贵在郊，其制不一，要之，内外皆有学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198455_comment'></div>贾谊按《大戴礼》，以谓礼有五学，盖本诸此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198455_comment'></div>历代唯唐贞观间，四夷皆遣子弟入学，国子监三学之士至八千人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198455_comment'></div>神宗皇帝元丰二年始立太学，立三舍，分命师儒，以教养天下之士，盖有志于成周之宾兴贤能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198455_comment'></div>臣面奉德音，诏天下皆兴学贡士，仍建外学于王国之南，待其岁考行艺，升之太学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198455_comment'></div>悉出陛下圣意，合于先王建学之制，而仰绍神宗皇帝之遗训，天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198455_comment'></div>今具外学条件如左：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1198455'>一、国子祭酒总治外学事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198455_comment'></div>今来既设外学，其官属欲增损，欲依下项人数立定员数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198455_comment'></div>缘太学生将来减少，拨入外学，内外分为两学，亦须量增官员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198455_comment'></div>今欲太学博士十二员，减六员为外学博士，增四员，通作十员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198455_comment'></div>太学正、录各五员，今欲减二员入外学，各增三员，通馀五员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198455_comment'></div>其馀职事人亦仿此增减。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1198455_comment'></div>外学官属：司业一人，丞一人，博士十人，学正五人，学录五人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1198455_comment'></div>职事人系学生充：学谕十人，直学二人，斋长每斋一人，斋谕每斋一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1198455_comment'></div>外舍生三千人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1198455_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1198455'>一、太学上舍一百人，内舍三百人。<div class='inline'
