id='poem_sentence_19_1198455_comment'></div>今诸路贡士既多，则上舍、内舍难拘旧额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1198455_comment'></div>欲候将来贡试到合格人，即增上舍作二百人，内舍作六百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1198455_comment'></div>处上舍于太学，处外舍于外学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1198455_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1198455'>一、外学置斋一百，讲堂四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1198455_comment'></div>每斋五间、三十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1198455_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1198455'>一、太学自讼斋，以待学生之不率教者，令移于外学别置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1198455_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1198455'>一、外学生，诸路贡到，并入外学，候依法考选校试合格，升之太学为上舍、内舍生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1198455_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1198455'>一、见今太学外舍生且令依旧法在太学，候将来外学成日别取指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1198455_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1198455'>一、外学并依太学敕、令、格、式施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1198455_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1198455'><span class='label'>按：</span>《群书考索》后集卷二八。又见《宋会要辑稿》职官二八之一五（第三册第二九七九页），《文献通考》卷四二，《宋史》卷一五七《选举志》三、卷一六五《职官志》五。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1198455_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年11月</a>　条具宗室合行事件。作品：条具宗室合行事件劄子。<div id='poem_1198456' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198456' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198456?labeling=true' target='_blank'>条具宗室合行事件劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁元年十一月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198456")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198456_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198456'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198456'>伏考宗室，在祖宗朝，制禄盖寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198456_comment'></div>至仁宗时，始除南班官，自率府副率凡五六迁遂至正任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198456_comment'></div>承平日久，皇支寖繁，神宗皇帝乃下诏书，别其亲疏，异其等杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198456_comment'></div>遂断自祖宗袒免亲罢补环卫之官，尽除班行名目；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198456_comment'></div>袒免以外，更不赐名授官，止许应举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198456_comment'></div>自熙宁至今，宗室人无官者已一千五百馀人，宗女之未嫁者亦千五百有奇，皆宣祖、太祖之裔，或有贫困失所者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198456_comment'></div>臣等伏考神宗诏书，盖为袒免既已赐名授官，若愿应举者，自当依进士法；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198456_comment'></div>其非袒免，既不赐名授官，故止令量试艺业，即推恩数，非若应进士举之难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198456_comment'></div>至于年长，累试不中，则又有特与推恩、量材录用之制，则随其材器收录尽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198456_comment'></div>至于世数稍远，及贫无依者，则又赐田存恤有差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198456_comment'></div>逮元祐纷更，废量试之法，改依进士科举之制，是以自熙宁至元符初，三十馀年，中科举者才二十馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198456_comment'></div>既废量试之法，亦未尝有以年长推恩者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198456_comment'></div>赐田之令，徒为虚文，虽有量给钱米之法，未能周济其乏，遂致宗室不能自给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198456_comment'></div>臣等谨追考神宗诏书，推原本旨，稽之往昔，增以当今所可行者，谨条具如左：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1198456'>一、非袒免亲，乃祖宗六世孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198456_comment'></div>伏请将上件服属宗室二十五以上者，今次许于礼部投状，试经义或律义一道，以文理稍通者为合格，分为两等，候至来春，附进士榜推恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198456_comment'></div>内文艺优长者，临时取旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1198456_comment'></div>其不能试，或试不中者，并赴礼部书家状，读律，别作一项奏名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1198456_comment'></div>今来止为前此未曾推广补考量试推恩之令，致使宗室无官者遂众，有此陈请，只作一时指挥，不为永法，今后自依熙宁诏书赐田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1198456_comment'></div>其田并于两京近辅、沿流州军，取应未卖官田物业拨充。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1198456_comment'></div>每州府各置宗室官庄，专差文武官各一员，与逐州通判同行管干，逐县兼管，仍置指使二员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1198456_comment'></div>每岁量入为出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1198456_comment'></div>宗女量给嫁资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1198456_comment'></div>仍立定则例，量支嫁娶丧葬之费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1198456_comment'></div>其逐州自今后，有没官田产物业，更不出卖，并拨入官庄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1198456_comment'></div>仍先于京西北路拨田一万顷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1198456_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1198456'>一、熙宁诏书，袒免以下许随处置产业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1198456_comment'></div>其出官即置田宅，一如外官之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1198456_comment'></div>盖以宗支寖广，其疏属理当听其外居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1198456_comment'></div>勘会宗室旧来在宫有出入之限，有不许外交之禁，宫门有讥察之令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1198456_comment'></div>今疏属外居，仅遍都下，出入无禁，交游不节，往往冒犯法禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1198456_comment'></div>伏请非袒免亲以下两世，欲分于西京、南京、近辅或沿流便近居止，各随州郡大小创置屋宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1198456_comment'></div>仍先自西京为始，每处置敦宗院，差文臣一员、武臣一员管干，参酌在京院法禁可施行者颁下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1198456_comment'></div>应无父母兄弟，见任将军副使以上官者，许令前去；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1198456_comment'></div>若有父母兄弟而愿去，或无而不愿者听从便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1198456_comment'></div>依外官赴任立法，量给舟船接人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1198456_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_1198456'>一、乞依神宗诏书，不拘世数，应宗子宗女尤贫失所者，伏请委所在州郡报明，量加存恤讫奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1198456_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1198456'>一、乞于两京置外宗正司官，掌业所在宗室，择宗室之贤者管勾外宗正事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1198456_comment'></div>仍自朝廷于本州通判职官内选差二人兼领丞簿，以主其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1198456_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_1198456'>一、乞随所在诸宫置学，添教授，立法教养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1198456_comment'></div>量试宗室，依熙宁文武官试出官法策试经义，中选者许令出官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1198456_comment'></div>若再试不中者，止许在宫院，使食其禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1198456_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1198456'>一、神考釐正宗室袒免非袒免，各立奏补子孙之法，独缌麻亲旧用国荫，自来未有荫孙以下明文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1198456_comment'></div>伏请依外官例，得补荫孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1198456_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_1198456'>一、旧制，宗室袒免亲参选，常许不拘名次陈乞指占差遣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1198456_comment'></div>非袒免亲，初选依条添差外，更不拘名次陈乞指占差遣一次，以后每到部，与升一年名次陈乞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1198456_comment'></div>今后宗室非袒免以下亲量试出官者，并各于员阙外添差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1198456_comment'></div>每大郡通属县不得过十人，中郡不得过七人，小郡不得过四人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1198456_comment'></div>候到任不签书本职公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1198456_comment'></div>如有本辖长贰或监司二人保奏，堪任釐务，方得供职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1198456_comment'></div>未釐务者，添支驿券，供给人从。</div><div id='poem_sentence_49_1198456_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1198456'><span class='label'>按：</span>《宋朝事实》卷八。又见《宋会要辑稿》帝系五之一五。第一册第一一九页、崇儒一之一、（第三册第二一六三页）职官二○之三四、（第三册第二八三七页）职官五七之五二（第四册第三六七七页），《文献通考》卷二五九。）据《宋会要辑稿》帝系五之一八原注云，蔡京此劄子共条具九事，诸书所收皆不全，而互有详略异同。兹将《宋会要辑稿》帝系五之一五、职官二○之三四所载附录于下，以资补充参考。帝系五之一五云：「奉承德音，谨追考神宗诏书，推原本旨，稽之往昔，增以当今所可行者，谨条具如左。如允所请，即乞付本司立法施行。一、自熙宁降诏已来，宗室量试之法中废不讲，至绍圣间始复讲之，所以预试应格之人至少，亦未曾有以年长特推恩者。宗室之无官者繇此甚众。今若俟其累试不中，然后录用，缘未尝教养，一旦峻责其艺能，则推恩之文，殆成虚设。况非袒免亲，乃祖宗六世孙，恩泽所加，谓宜稍厚。乞将上件服属宗室年二十五已上者，今次许于礼部投状，试经义或律义二道，以文理稍通者为合格，分为两等，候至来春附进士榜推恩。内文艺优长者，临时取旨。其不能试，或试不中者，并赴礼部书家状，读律，别作一项奏名。只作一时指挥，不为永法，今后自依熙宁诏书并元符试法施行。一、宗室有世数既远，出仕外官者渐众，而宗女随夫之官者数亦不少。或亡殁于外任，而其子孙不能归葬，或随侍在外，因而流落，或孤寡无依，或道路贫病，若不存恤，恐无所归。今请委所在州军常切体量，如有上件宗室，仰随所在保明，量加存恤。乞奏其存恤格，从本司评议颁下。若应保奏而不保奏，或保奏而不以实，并杖一百。听宗室随所在监司陈述，监司依格给讫，按劾以闻。一、宗子虽有教授，名存实废。宗子往往不出听读。虽设宗子学，聚而为一，则有赴学之费、往来之劳，其势必不能群处。今请逐宫各置大小二学，添置教授二员。量立考选法，月书季考，取其文艺可称、不戾规矩者注于籍。在外住而愿入宫学者听。依熙宁诏书、元符试法量试推恩。其学制从本司参定。愿入太学律学者亦听。应宗子年十岁已上入小学，二十以上入大学，年不及而愿入者听从便。若无故应入学而不入，或应听读而不听读者，罚俸一月，再犯勒住朝参，三犯移自讼斋。即两人不入学，本官、本位尊长罚俸半月；三人以上并犯者罚一月，十人以上罚两月，重者申宗正司奏裁。一、今虽置学立师，为量试之法，然所学未广，遽使出长入治，必未能守法奉令，而至瘝官废职。伏请依熙宁文武官试出官法再试经义，中选者许令出官。若再试不中者，止许在宫院，使食其禄。其试法从本司参定。一、熙宁间神宗釐正宗室，乃有袒免亲赐名授官，非袒免亲更不赐名授官，只许应举之制。袒免、非袒免亦各立奏补子孙之法。独缌麻亲旧用国荫，自来未有荫孙已下明文。今请依外官例，得补荫孙。一、旧制，宗室袒免亲初参选，常许不拘名次陈乞指占差遣。非袒免亲初参选，依条添差外，更许不拘名次陈乞指占差遣一次。以后每到部，如无遗阙，与升一年名次。今来袒免以下亲出官者，人数寖多，侵占在部元阙不少。缘职事既有修废，若不分别勤怠，无以劝沮，欲乞今后应宗室非袒免以下亲，量试出外官者，并各于员阙外添差。每大郡通都属县不得过十人，中郡不得过七人，小郡不得过四人。到任不签书本职公事。如有本辖长贰或监司二人保奏，堪任釐务，方得供职；未釐务者，添支驿券，供给人从并减半支破。」职官二○之三四云：「追考神宗诏书，条具宗室事当今可行者，乞付本司立法。一、袒免外，两世贫无官者，既不赐官，又不量试，故熙宁诏书惟赐田土。此服属既尽，而恩有不可已者也。今宗室未食禄者，与夫宗女未嫁者甚众，世数既远，禄不可及，乞依熙宁诏书赐田。其田并于两京近辅、沿流州军取应未卖官田物业拨充。每州府各置宗室官庄，转差文武官各一员，与逐州通判同行管干。逐县仰县兼管，仍差指使二员。所收钱物并付系省仓库收贮，每岁量入为出，常于三分内桩留一分，以待水旱，约服属远近，每月量支俸料。宗女量给嫁资，仍立定则例，量支婚嫁丧葬之费。其逐州自今后应有没官田产物业，更不出卖，并拨入官庄。其管干官并指使并增俸料。若能擘画增衍，量立赏典；或致亏欠，亦立罚格。仍先于京西北路拨田一万顷，并从本司立法行下。一、宗室旧来在宫有出入之限，有不许外交之禁，宫门有机（按：应作「讥」，下同。）察之义（按：「义」字当衍。）令。今疏属外居。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1198456_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年12月</a>　乞荊湖等七路茶依舊禁榷。作品：乞荊湖等七路茶依舊禁榷奏。<div id='poem_1198457' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198457' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198457?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞荆湖等七路茶依旧禁榷奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁元年十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198457")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198457_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198457'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198457'>荆湖南北、江南东西、淮南、两浙、福建七路产茶，自乾德二年立法禁榷，官置场收买，许商贾就京师榷货务纳钱给钞，赴十三山场六榷货务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198457_comment'></div>至祥符中，岁收息五百馀万缗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198457_comment'></div>庆历以来，法制寖坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198457_comment'></div>嘉祐初，遂罢禁榷，行便商之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198457_comment'></div>客人园户私相贸易，公私不给，利源寖销，岁入不过八十馀万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198457_comment'></div>元丰中，先帝尝命有司讲求，而法废已久，议者不能上承圣志，议未及行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198457_comment'></div>窃考在昔茶法之弊，盖缘科配人户，不计丰凶，州县催迫，人多逃避，嘉祐改法，指以为说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198457_comment'></div>今欲将荆湖、江、淮、两浙、福建七路州军所产茶，依旧禁榷，选官置司，提举措置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198457_comment'></div>并于产茶州县随处置场，官为收买，更不于人户税上科纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198457_comment'></div>禁客人与园户私相交易，所置场处，委官籍记园户姓名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198457_comment'></div>所有置场茶本钱，欲降度牒二千道、末盐钞二百万贯，更特于逐路朝廷诸色封桩钱、并坊场常平剩钱内共借四十万贯，共三百万贯，令逐路分擘充买茶本钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198457_comment'></div>差官分路措置：湖南、北路欲差一员，江东、西路欲差一员，淮南、两浙路欲差一员，福建路欲差一员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198457_comment'></div>将来措置就绪，即共差都大提举七路茶事二员总之，馀官并罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198457_comment'></div>其勾集园户，籍会户数，酌量年例所出，约人户可卖之数，年终立为茶额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198457_comment'></div>所有复行禁榷条法，检会大中祥符所行旧法，并庆历后来私贩害公之弊，取今日可行者酌中修立，接续为法，颁降施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1198457_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　乞以河北京东末盐通至陕西。作品：乞以河北京东末盐通至陕西奏。<div id='poem_1198458' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198458' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198458?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞以河北京东末盐通至陕西奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁初）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198458")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198458_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198458'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198458'>河北、京东末盐，客运至京及京西，袋输官钱六千，而盐本不及一千，施行未久，收息及二百万缗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198458_comment'></div>如通至陕西，其利必倍。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1198458_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年1月</a>　二年正月，进左仆射。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年1月</a>　进诸州县学敕令格式。作品：进诸州县学敕令格式状。<div id='poem_1198459' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198459' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198459?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进诸州县学敕令格式状<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁二年一月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1103年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198459")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198459_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198459'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198459'>昨具陈请，乞诸路置学养士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198459_comment'></div>伏奉诏令讲议立法，修立成诸州县学敕令格式并一时指挥，凡一十三册，谨缮写上进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198459_comment'></div>如得允当，乞下本司镂版颁行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1198459_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年2月</a>　陕西转运副使许天启申送到新铸铜、铁钱样。作品：陕西铸钱事奏。<div id='poem_1198460' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198460' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198460?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陕西铸钱事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁二年二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1103年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198460")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198460_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198460'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198460'>据陕西转运副使许天启申送到新铸铜、铁钱样。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198460_comment'></div>已降指挥，铜钱于岁终须管铸二十万贯，铁钱铸二百万贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198460_comment'></div>自来铸钱，张官置吏，招刺军兵，所费不少，而军兵之役，最为辛苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198460_comment'></div>官得至薄，率三钱得一钱之利，盖是久失擘画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198460_comment'></div>今陕西、河中府等处，民间私铸最多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198460_comment'></div>召募私铸人，令赴官充铸钱工匠，广为营屋，许其一家之人在营居止，不必限其出入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198460_comment'></div>官给物料，尽其一家人力鼓铸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198460_comment'></div>计其工直，率十分中支若干分数充其工价。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198460_comment'></div>又可收私铸人在官，盖昔人招天下亡命即山铸钱之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198460_comment'></div>欲令许天启相度，疾速准此施行，仍与旧来军工相兼鼓铸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198460_comment'></div>今来所铸铜钱除陕西、四川、河东系铁钱地分更不得行使外，诸路并令折十行用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198460_comment'></div>其钱唯令陕西铁钱地分铸造，却于铜钱地分行使，贵绝私铸之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198460_comment'></div>如有私铸，并以一文计小钱十科罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198460_comment'></div>又陕西铜钱至重，每一钱当铁钱三或四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198460_comment'></div>今夹锡铸造，样制精好，欲一钱当铜钱二支用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198460_comment'></div>令许天启相度，依此施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1198460_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年3月</a>　农田水利等所用钱由常平司支给。作品：农田水利等所用钱由常平司支给劄子。<div id='poem_1198461' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198461' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198461?labeling=true' target='_blank'>农田水利等所用钱由常平司支给劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁二年三月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1103年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198461")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198461_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198461'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198461'>农田、水利、山泽、市易、抵当皆常平职事，悉以利民，所用钱物合支常平息钱，仰提举常平司审量支给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198461_comment'></div>一万贯石以上申尚书户部，限三日行下支给。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1198461_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年3月</a>　请复修水土之政。作品：请复修水土之政奏。<div id='poem_1198462' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198462' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198462?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请复修水土之政奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁二年三月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1103年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198462")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198462_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198462'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198462'>熙宁之初，修水土之政，行市易之法，兴山泽之利，皆王政之大者，追述缉熙，当在今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198462_comment'></div>农田如荒闲可耕凿，瘠卤可变膏腴，陆可为水，水可为陆之类；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198462_comment'></div>水利如陂塘可修，灌溉可复，积潦可泄，圩堤可兴之类；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198462_comment'></div>山泽如铜、铅、金、银、铁、锡、水银坑冶，及林木可养，斤斧可禁，山荒可种植之类，县并置丞一员，以掌其事。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1198462_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年9月</a>　天宁节请赐天下寺额。作品：天宁节请赐天下寺额奏。<div id='poem_1198463' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198463' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198463?labeling=true' target='_blank'>天宁节请赐天下寺额奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁二年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1103年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198463")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198463_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198463'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198463'>臣等伏以陛下遹追先烈，分别邪正，明信赏罚，上当天心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198463_comment'></div>今天宁届，伏请天下州军各赐寺额，以崇宁为名，上祝睿算。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1198463_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年2月</a>　进六尚局敕令格式。作品：进六尚局敕令格式状。<div id='poem_1198464' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198464' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198464?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进六尚局敕令格式状<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁三年二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198464")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198464_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198464'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198464'>奉诏令讲议司修立六尚局条约闻奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198464_comment'></div>谨以元陈请画一事件，并稽考参酌，创为约束，删润修立，成殿中省提举所六尚局供奉库敕、令、格、式并看详共六十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198464_comment'></div>内不可著为永法者存为申明，事干两局以上者总为殿中省通用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198464_comment'></div>仍冠以崇宁为名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198464_comment'></div>所有应干条画起请、续降申明，及合用旧司条法，已系新书编载者更不行用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198464_comment'></div>不系新书收载，各合依旧引用。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1198464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1198464'><span class='label'>按：</span>《宋会要辑稿》职官一九之九（第三册第二八一五页）。又见同书刑法一之二二（第七册第六四七二页）。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1198464_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年4月</a>　罢讲议司。作品：讲议司罢局奏。<div id='poem_1198465' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198465' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198465?labeling=true' target='_blank'>讲议司罢局奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁三年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198465")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198465_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198465'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198465'>奉诏置司讲议法度，更历岁年，曾不足仰称委任之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198465_comment'></div>今文字不多，理当归之省部，付于有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198465_comment'></div>乞限一月结局，其未了事件送尚书省分隶施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1198465_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年7月</a>　进呈崇宁方田敕令格式。作品：进呈崇宁方田敕令格式劄子。<div id='poem_1198466' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198466' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198466?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进呈崇宁方田敕令格式劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁三年七月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198466")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198466_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198466'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198466'>臣等窃以赋调之不平久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198466_comment'></div>自开阡陌，使民得以田私相贸易，富者贪于有馀，厚立价以规利；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198466_comment'></div>贫者迫于不足，薄移税以速售。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198466_comment'></div>故富有跨州轶县，所管者莫非膏腴，而赋调反轻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198466_comment'></div>贫者所存无几，又且瘠薄，而赋调反重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198466_comment'></div>因循至今，其弊愈甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198466_comment'></div>熙宁初，神宗皇帝灼见此弊，遂诏有司讲究方田利害，作法而推行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198466_comment'></div>盖以土色肥瘠别田之美恶，定赋之多寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198466_comment'></div>方为之帐，而步亩高下丈尺不可隐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198466_comment'></div>户给之帖，而升合尺寸无所遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198466_comment'></div>以卖买，则民不能容其巧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198466_comment'></div>以催收，则吏不能措其奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198466_comment'></div>邦财自此丰，民赋自此省，其为法岂小补哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198466_comment'></div>五路州县有经方田者，至今公私以为利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198466_comment'></div>遭元祐纷更，美意良法未遍于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198466_comment'></div>今其文籍见在，可举而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1198466_comment'></div>今检会熙宁《方田敕》，推广神考法意，删去重复，冲改，取其应行者为《方田法》，计九册，以《崇宁方田敕令格式》为名，谨具进呈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1198466_comment'></div>如允所奏，乞付三省颁降施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1198466_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年8月</a>　八月，作大晟乐。以蔡攸提举大成府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年6月</a>　书元佑党籍碑。作品：元祐党籍碑。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《长编纪事本末》作崇宁三年六月壬戌所奏。）</span><div id='poem_1198518' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198518' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198518?labeling=true' target='_blank'>元祐党籍碑<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁三年六月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198518")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198518_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198518'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198518'>皇帝嗣位之五年，旌别淑慝，明信赏刑，黜元祐害政之臣，靡有佚罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198518_comment'></div>乃命有司夷考罪状，第其首恶，与其附丽者以闻，得三百九人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198518_comment'></div>皇帝书而刊之石，置于文德殿门之东壁，永为万世臣子之戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198518_comment'></div>又诏臣京书之，将以颁之天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198518_comment'></div>臣窃惟陛下仁圣英武，遵制扬功，彰善瘅恶，以昭先烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198518_comment'></div>臣敢不对扬休命，仰承陛下孝悌继述之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198518_comment'></div>司空、尚书左仆射兼门下侍郎臣蔡京谨书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1198518_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年11月</a>　更定神宗皇帝徽号。作品：更定神宗皇帝徽号册文。<div id='poem_1198419' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198419' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198419?labeling=true' target='_blank'>更定神宗皇帝徽号册文<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁三年十一月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198419")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198419_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198419'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198419'>孝子嗣皇帝臣佶谨稽首再拜言：臣闻自古在昔，作之君师，立政造事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198419_comment'></div>圣有所生，王有所成，盛德大业，暴白当世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198419_comment'></div>或放于功而曰勋，或协于帝而曰华，或可名于大，或可名于小，虽出人心，亦天所命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198419_comment'></div>至若名不偕于功，言不顺于事，遏佚前人之光，惟厥后嗣，罔敢庸释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198419_comment'></div>末予冲人，奉承大统，克笃先烈，率时昭考，念无以报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198419_comment'></div>而乃者群臣所上，典策所称，绍天之命，法古而治，功始建而未成于功，德以运而非运于德，大惧不足以骏惠在天之灵，慰神明之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198419_comment'></div>窃迹先王运量四海，体元以统天，显道以应世，以德而帝，以业而王，非至神其孰能与于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198419_comment'></div>惟我神考，以上圣之材，接百王之绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198419_comment'></div>典谟所载，风雅所歌，本数末度，述而作之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198419_comment'></div>放黜嵬琐，与时变通，作新斯人，更法定令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198419_comment'></div>正身齐家，小大祗若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198419_comment'></div>外薄四海，罔有不钦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198419_comment'></div>藏固于密，无能名焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198419_comment'></div>然验诸猷为，形容拟议，则而象之，可考而言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198419_comment'></div>资始于乾，资生于坤，弗违于天，而为之先，合气于汉，而原其本，首出庶物，以体于元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198419_comment'></div>神而明之，大而化之，列而在事，陈而为法，缉熙光明，以显于道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1198419_comment'></div>钦明文思，浚哲温恭，以身为度，表正万邦，帝德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1198419_comment'></div>九功为叙，九叙为歌，有典有则，贻厥子孙，王功也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1198419_comment'></div>恭惟神宗皇帝备道全美，其大若此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1198419_comment'></div>追既往之未究，伸孝思之罔极，举是四者，丕扬显烈，合并旧章，于是为称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1198419_comment'></div>今燎禋泰坛，戒事有日，率吁众志，申命自天，对越祖宗，昭示万世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1198419_comment'></div>谨遣司空、尚书左仆射兼门下侍郎、上柱国、嘉国公、食邑五千八百户、食实封一千六百户蔡京奉玉册玉宝，上徽号曰体元显道帝德王功英文烈武钦仁圣孝皇帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1198419_comment'></div>伏惟灵德在上，临下有赫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1198419_comment'></div>昭受明命，绥我思成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1198419_comment'></div>永世有辞，克昌厥后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1198419_comment'></div>谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1198419_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1198419'><span class='label'>按：</span>《宋会要辑稿》礼五八之五二（第二册第一六三七页。）<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1198419_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年11月</a>　增上哲宗皇帝徽号。作品：增上哲宗皇帝徽号册文。<div id='poem_1198420' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198420' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198420?labeling=true' target='_blank'>增上哲宗皇帝徽号册文<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁三年十一月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198420")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198420_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198420'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198420'>孝弟嗣皇帝臣佶谨稽首再拜言：臣闻昔者明王崇德广业，举而措之天下，日见之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198420_comment'></div>于用则藏，于仁则显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198420_comment'></div>其称名或小，其取类则大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198420_comment'></div>故令闻广誉，克有辞于永世，无得而加焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198420_comment'></div>乃若德有馀于业，名不称其实，未足以丕扬显烈，以端命于上帝，则在我后之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198420_comment'></div>恭惟哲宗钦文睿武昭孝皇帝，仁覆四海，十有六年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198420_comment'></div>肆其即位，越在冲幼，沉潜刚克，以蒙养正，动静有度，不大声色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198420_comment'></div>左右仆御侍从之臣，亦罔能知，盖不言者九年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198420_comment'></div>爰及亲政，率时昭考，永言孝思，追悼先烈，弗克钦若，溃于厥成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198420_comment'></div>放逐奸宄，是正诋诬，遵制扬功，仪刑典则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198420_comment'></div>登用善良，协于克一，四方风动，如日之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198420_comment'></div>至于清静而寡欲，体仁而继善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198420_comment'></div>先后天时，遇灾而惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198420_comment'></div>遵者贵德，靡所不钦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198420_comment'></div>南面而听，尊严若神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198420_comment'></div>瘅恶虽弗容贷，而好善常若不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1198420_comment'></div>故小大祗若，无侮无拂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1198420_comment'></div>市无剖斗折衡之争，朝无错立族谈之犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1198420_comment'></div>慈故能勇，外攘夷狄，开辟境土，克继前人，卒其武功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1198420_comment'></div>皇天眷佑，诸福毕至，地不爱宝，神玺自出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1198420_comment'></div>英声茂实，莫可殚穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1198420_comment'></div>末予冲人，祗奉顾托，付以大业，夙夜祗慄，惧弗能胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1198420_comment'></div>乃者奸臣乘隙，覆出为恶，公肆抵戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1198420_comment'></div>用正典刑，无有佚罚，显谟丕烈，既晦而明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1198420_comment'></div>然其垂之将来，昭示无极，其敢不虔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1198420_comment'></div>爰卜日至，禋于圜丘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1198420_comment'></div>褒对明神，增备徽典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1198420_comment'></div>稽诸故实，协于师言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1198420_comment'></div>自天申锡，万邦作孚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1198420_comment'></div>谨遣金紫光禄大夫、知枢密院事、上柱国、南阳郡开国公、食邑三千三百户、食实封八百户蔡卞，奉玉册玉宝，上徽号曰哲宗宪元继道显德定功钦文睿武齐圣昭孝皇帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1198420_comment'></div>恭惟在天之灵，降鉴于下，来燕来宁，膺受兹礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1198420_comment'></div>于昭于天，俾缉熙于纯嘏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1198420_comment'></div>谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1198420_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年11月</a>　乞以幸辟雍手诏模勒刊石。作品：乞以幸辟雍手诏模勒刊石奏。<div id='poem_1198467' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198467' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198467?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞以幸辟雍手诏模勒刊石奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁三年十一月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198467")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198467_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198467'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198467'>伏睹车驾临幸辟雍，亲书手诏面赐国子司业吴絪等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198467_comment'></div>乞下有司模勒刊石，颁赐诸路州学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198467_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1198467_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年</a>　调整开封府职官。作品：开封府职官奏。<div id='poem_1198468' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198468' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198468?labeling=true' target='_blank'>开封府职官奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁三年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198468")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198468_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198468'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198468'>乞罢权知府，置牧一员、尹一员，专总府事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198468_comment'></div>少尹二员，分左右，贰府之政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198468_comment'></div>牧以皇子领之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198468_comment'></div>尹以文臣充，在六曹尚书之下、侍郎之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198468_comment'></div>少尹在左右司郎官之下、列曹郎官之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198468_comment'></div>以士、户、仪、兵、刑、工为六曹次序，司录二员，六曹各二员，参军事八员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198468_comment'></div>开封、祥符两县置案仿此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198468_comment'></div>易胥吏之称，略依《唐六典》制度。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1198468_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年7月</a>　建议设定四辅郡区划及职官。作品：四辅郡区划及职官奏。<div id='poem_1198469' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198469' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198469?labeling=true' target='_blank'>四辅郡区划及职官奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁四年七月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198469")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198469_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198469'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198469'>伏奉圣旨，京畿四面可置辅郡，屏卫京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198469_comment'></div>谨酌地远近之中，割移县镇，分置四辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198469_comment'></div>南以颍昌府为南辅，割汝州之郏县隶之，凡七县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198469_comment'></div>东去南京道里差远，今以襄邑县建名辅州，为东辅，割南京宁陵、楚丘、柘城、京畿之考城、太康隶之，凡六县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198469_comment'></div>西以郑州为西辅，割西京密县隶之，凡六县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198469_comment'></div>北以澶州为北辅，割北京朝城、南乐隶之，凡七县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198469_comment'></div>四辅郡并依节度州，以大中大夫以上充知州事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198469_comment'></div>置副总管、钤辖各一员，知州都总管，馀依三路帅臣法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198469_comment'></div>各屯马步军共二万人，积贮粮草，每州五百万。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1198469_comment'></div></div></div><br />年份未详　崇寜中蔡京等修哲宗史为王安石传。作品：王安石传。<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁中蔡京等修哲宗史为王安石传至以安石为圣人。朱熹《三朝名臣言行録》三朝名臣言行後録卷第七 143。）</span><div id='poem_1198517' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198517' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198517?labeling=true' target='_blank'>王安石传</a><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198517")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198517_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198517'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198517'>自先王泽竭，国异家殊，由汉迄唐，源流浸深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198517_comment'></div>宋兴，文物盛矣，然不知道德性命之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198517_comment'></div>安石奋乎百世之下，追尧、舜、三代，通乎昼夜阴阳所不能测，而入于神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198517_comment'></div>初著《杂说》数万言，世谓其言与孟轲相上下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198517_comment'></div>于是天下之士始原道德之意，窥性命之端云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1198517_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1198517'><span class='label'>按：</span>。衢本《郡斋读书志》卷一二「王氏杂说」条，光绪十年长沙王氏刊本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1198517_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年2月</a>　二月，蔡京罢相。授守司空、开府仪同三司、安远军节度使、中太一宫使，进封魏国公。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年1月</a>　正月，蔡京复相，为尚书左仆射兼门下侍郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年7月</a>　修成馬遞鋪敕令格式。作品：修成马递铺敕令格式状。<div id='poem_1198470' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198470' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198470?labeling=true' target='_blank'>修成马递铺敕令格式状<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观元年七月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1107年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198470")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198470_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198470'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198470'>伏奉圣旨，令尚书省重修马递铺海行法颁行诸路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198470_comment'></div>臣奉承圣训，删润旧文，编缵成书，共为一法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198470_comment'></div>谨修成敕、令、格、式、申明、对修总三十卷，并看详七十卷，共一百册，计六复，随状上进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198470_comment'></div>如或可行，乞降付三省镂版颁降施行，仍乞以《大观马递铺敕令格式》为名。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1198470_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年9月</a>　加上僖祖皇帝徽号。作品：加上僖祖皇帝徽号册文。<div id='poem_1198421' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198421' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198421?labeling=true' target='_blank'>加上僖祖皇帝徽号册文<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观元年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1107年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198421")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198421_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198421'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198421'>孝曾孙嗣皇帝臣佶谨再拜稽首言：臣闻在昔先王奄宅天下，敷遗后人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198421_comment'></div>嗣有令绪，推而上之，逮厥本初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198421_comment'></div>惟我有宋艺祖文考，顾諟明命，抚绥万邦，道洽政治，垂百五十年于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198421_comment'></div>社稷宗庙，罔不祗肃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198421_comment'></div>远迩内外，罔不率俾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198421_comment'></div>原其所自，本乎上世，权舆万事，贻燕所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198421_comment'></div>盖惟我僖祖皇帝潜德训行，遵养时晦，迈迹自身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198421_comment'></div>上帝顾歆，克昌厥后，贻厥子孙，诞受多方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198421_comment'></div>率乃祖之攸行，格于皇天，以迄于今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198421_comment'></div>施及寡昧，祗受休烈，迪惟前人，光施于后，罔敢遏佚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198421_comment'></div>丕釐九庙之制，若稽于古，万世不祧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198421_comment'></div>惟厥名称，率由故常，未克丕显，夙夜祗慄，惧弗克称，用请命于上帝，诞扬典册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198421_comment'></div>夫以真治身，以绪应世，由之以行，因之以著，之谓立道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198421_comment'></div>王之所成，业之所兴，以有家邦，以造区夏，之谓肇基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198421_comment'></div>不显乎世，不成乎名，始于笃实，终以光辉，此德之所积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198421_comment'></div>居而有之，作邦作对，佑我后裔，无竞维烈，此功之所起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1198421_comment'></div>经纬其道，饰设其用，隐而不辉，以懿其文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1198421_comment'></div>沉潜刚克，载用有嗣，式遏乱略，以宪其武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1198421_comment'></div>致虚以明，允执其中，是谓睿和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1198421_comment'></div>以假有庙，保世滋大，是谓至孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1198421_comment'></div>合是众美，以形容盛德，肆冒闻于上下神祇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1198421_comment'></div>谨遣册宝使、司空、尚书左仆射、门下侍郎、上柱国、魏国公、食邑八千二百户、食实封二千六百户蔡京，奉玉册玉宝，加上徽号曰立道肇基积德起功懿文宪武睿和至孝皇帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1198421_comment'></div>以迪我祖考，追孝奉先之心，慰在天之神，严庙祏之奉，昭示万世，承天之休无斁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1198421_comment'></div>谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1198421_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年9月</a>　乞以方轸弹章付有司推究事实。作品：乞以方轸弹章付有司推究事实劄子。<div id='poem_1198471' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198471' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198471?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞以方轸弹章付有司推究事实劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观元年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1107年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198471")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198471_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198471'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198471'>伏蒙宣示方轸章疏一项，论列臣：「睥睨社稷，内怀不道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198471_comment'></div>效王莽自立为司空，效曹操自立为魏国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198471_comment'></div>视祖宗神灵为无物，玩陛下不啻若婴儿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198471_comment'></div>专以绍述熙丰之说为自媒之计，上以不孝劫持人主，下以谤讪诋诬恐赫天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198471_comment'></div>威震人主，祸移生灵，风声气焰，中外畏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198471_comment'></div>大臣保家族不敢议，小臣保寸禄不敢言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198471_comment'></div>颠倒纪纲，肆意妄作，自古为臣之奸，未有如京今日为甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198471_comment'></div>爰自崇宁已来，交通阍寺，通谒宫禁，蠹国用则若粪土，轻名器以市私恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198471_comment'></div>内自执政侍从，外至帅臣监司，无非京之亲戚门人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198471_comment'></div>政事上不合于天心，下悉结于民怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198471_comment'></div>若设九鼎，铸大钱，置三卫，兴三舍，祭天地于西郊，如此之类，非独无益，又且无补，其意安在？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198471_comment'></div>京凡妄作，必持说劫持上下曰『此先帝之法也』，『此三代之法也』，或曰『熙、丰遗意，未及施行』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198471_comment'></div>仰惟神考十九年间，典章文物，粲然大备，岂蔡京不得驰聘于当年，必欲妄施于今日，以罔在天之神灵？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198471_comment'></div>凡欲奏请，尽乞作御笔指挥行出，语士大夫曰：『此上意也』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198471_comment'></div>明日或降指挥，更不施行，则又语人曰：『京实启之也』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198471_comment'></div>善则称己，过则称君，必欲陛下敛天下怨而后已，是岂宗社之福乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1198471_comment'></div>天下之事无常是，亦无常非，可则因之，否则革之，惟其当之为贵，何必三代之为哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1198471_comment'></div>李唐三百年间，所传者二十一君，所可称者太宗一人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1198471_comment'></div>当时如房、杜、王、魏，智虑才识必不在蔡京之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1198471_comment'></div>窃观贞观间，未尝一言以及三代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1198471_comment'></div>后世论太宗之治者则曰：除隋之乱，比迹汤、武，致治之美，庶几成、康，自古功德兼隆，由汉以来，未之有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1198471_comment'></div>京不学无术，妄以三代之说欺陛下，岂不为有识者之所笑也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1198471_comment'></div>元丰三年，废殿前廨宇二千四百六十间，造尚书省，分六曹，设二十四司，以总天下机务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1198471_comment'></div>落成之日，车驾亲幸，命有司立法，诸门墙窗壁辄增修改易者徒贰年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1198471_comment'></div>京恶白虎地不利宰相，尽命毁坼，收置禁中，是欲利陛下乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1198471_comment'></div>是谓之『绍述』乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1198471_comment'></div>括地数千里，屯兵数十万，建置四辅郡，遣亲信门人为四辅州总管，又以宋乔年为京畿转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1198471_comment'></div>密讽兖州父老诣阙下，请车驾登封，意在为东京留守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1198471_comment'></div>是欲乘舆一动，投间窃发，呼吸群助，不知宗庙社稷何所依倚？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1198471_comment'></div>陛下将措圣躬于何地？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1198471_comment'></div>臣尝中夜思之，不觉涕泗横流也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1198471_comment'></div>臣闻京建议立方田法，欲扰安业百姓，借使行之，岂不召乱乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1198471_comment'></div>又况数年间行盐钞法，朝行夕改，昔是今非，以此脱赚客旅财物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1198471_comment'></div>道途行旅谓朝廷法令信如寒暑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1198471_comment'></div>未行旬浃，又报盐法变矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1198471_comment'></div>钞为故纸，为无物，家财荡尽，赴水自缢，客死异乡，孤儿寡妇，号泣吁天者不知其几千万人，闻者为之伤心，见者为之流涕，生灵怨叹，皆归咎于陛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1198471_comment'></div>然京自谓暴虐无伤，奈皇天后土之有灵乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1198471_comment'></div>所幸者，祖宗不驰一骑以得天下，仁厚之德，涵养生灵，几二百年矣，四方之民不忍生事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1198471_comment'></div>万一有垄上之耕夫，等死之亭长，啸聚亡命于一方，天下向应，不约而从，陛下何以枝梧其祸乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1198471_comment'></div>内外臣僚皆京亲戚门人，将谁为陛下使乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1198471_comment'></div>京乘此时，谈笑可得陛下之天下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1198471_comment'></div>元符末年，陛下嗣服之初，忠臣义士明目张胆，思见太平，投匦以陈己见者无日无之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1198471_comment'></div>京钳天下之口，欲塞陛下耳目，分为邪等，贼虐忠良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1198471_comment'></div>天下之士皆以忠义为羞，方且全身远害之不暇，何暇救陛下之失乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1198471_comment'></div>奈何陛下以京为忠贯星日，以忠臣义士为谤讪诋诬，或流配远方，或除名编置，或不许齿仕籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1198471_comment'></div>以言得罪者无虑万人矣，谁肯为陛下言哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1198471_comment'></div>蔡攸者，垂髫一<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1198471", 1198471, "Clauses/177/Comments/0")'>顽童</span>耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1198471_comment'></div>京遣攸日与陛下游从嬉戏，必无文武尧舜之道启沃陛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1198471_comment'></div>惟以花㘽怪石，笼禽槛兽，舟车相衔，不绝道路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1198471_comment'></div>今日所献者则曰臣攸上进，明日所献者则又曰臣攸上进，故欲愚陛下，使之不知天下治乱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1198471_comment'></div>久虚谏院不差人，自除门人为御史，京有反状，陛下何从而知？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1198471_comment'></div>臣是以知京必反也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1198471_comment'></div>臣与京皆壶山人也，案谶云：『水绕壶公山，此时方好看』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1198471_comment'></div>京讽部使者凿渠以绕山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1198471_comment'></div>日者星文谪见西方，日蚀正阳之月，天意所以启陛下聪明者可谓极也，奈何陛下略不省悔默悟？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1198471_comment'></div>帝意止于肆恩赦，开寺观，避正殿，减常膳，举常仪，以答天戒而已；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1198471_comment'></div>然国贼尚全首领，未闻枭首以谢天下百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1198471_comment'></div>此则神民共愤，祖宗含怒在天之日久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1198471_comment'></div>陛下勿谓雉鸣乎鼎，榖生于朝，不害高宗、太戊之德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1198471_comment'></div>九年之水，七年之旱，不害尧、汤之圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1198471_comment'></div>古人之事出于适然，今日之事祸发不测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1198471_comment'></div>天象人情，危慄如是，伏惟陛下留神听览，念艺祖创业之难，思履霜坚冰之戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1198471_comment'></div>今日冰已坚矣，非独履霜之渐，愿陛下早图之，后悔之何及！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1198471_comment'></div>臣批肝为纸，沥血书辞，忘万死，叩天阍，区区为陛下力言者，非慕陛下爵禄而言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1198471_comment'></div>所可重者祖宗之庙社，所可惜者天下之生灵，而自忘其言之迫切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1198471_comment'></div>陛下杀之可也，赦之可也，窜之可也，臣一死生，不系于重轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1198471_comment'></div>陛下上体天戒，下顾人言，安可爱一国贼，而忘庙社生灵之重乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1198471_comment'></div>冒渎天威，无任战慄之至，谨备录如后」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1198471_comment'></div>臣读之骇汗，若无所容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1198471_comment'></div>臣以愚陋备位宰司，不能镇伏纪纲，讫无毫发报称，徒致奸言干浼圣听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1198471_comment'></div>且人臣有将必诛之刑，告言不实有反坐之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1198471_comment'></div>臣若有是事，死不敢辞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1198471_comment'></div>臣若无是事，方轸之言不可不辩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1198471_comment'></div>伏望圣慈付之有司，推究事实，不可不问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1198471_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_74_1198471_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年10月</a>　乞以皇帝诚孝感天久雨忽霁事付史馆。作品：乞以皇帝诚孝感天久雨忽霁事付史馆奏。<div id='poem_1198472' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198472' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198472?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞以皇帝诚孝感天久雨忽霁事付史馆奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观元年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1107年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198472")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198472_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198472'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198472'>伏见宗祀之月，久雨不霁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198472_comment'></div>宿斋之夕，雨尚滂注。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198472_comment'></div>翌日，陛下登辂启行，自宫诣庙，天日清明，和气充塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198472_comment'></div>既至庙门，却伞去扇，进辇弗御，步入斋殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198472_comment'></div>及祼献神宗室，涕洟欷歔，感动左右；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198472_comment'></div>再行奠币，泪犹不止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198472_comment'></div>诚孝昭格，天人感通，乞付史馆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1198472_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1198472'><span class='label'>按：</span>《宋会要辑稿》礼一七之一六（第一册第六九四页）。又见同书礼二四之五七（第一册第九二八页）。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1198472_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年12月</a>　以广南西路夜郎、康居之属纳土，加蔡京太尉。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年1月</a>　正月，蔡京进太师。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年3月</a>　三月，以复洮州功，赐蔡京玉带。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年9月</a>　西南蛮夷纳土。作品：西南蛮夷纳土奏。<div id='poem_1198473' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198473' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198473?labeling=true' target='_blank'>西南蛮夷纳土奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观二年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1108年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198473")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198473_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198473'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198473'>据黔南等路奏：安化上三州一镇山河土地尽献纳朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198473_comment'></div>上州周围三千五百馀里，户一万，人六万五千，永为王民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198473_comment'></div>又思广峒蒙光明等献纳土地，周围计一千五百里，户八百，人九千馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198473_comment'></div>又落安知峒程大法等献地，周围二千五百里，户八千，人四万五千馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198473_comment'></div>又都丹团黄光明献纳土地，周围二千馀里，户七千馀，人四万馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198473_comment'></div>以上计五万一千一百馀户，二十六万二千馀人，幅员二万九千馀里，各款塞听命，已相度列置州县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198473_comment'></div>又据靖州西道路诸蛮杨再立，献纳土地二百七十五人，计七状，周围三千馀里，户四千五百，人一万一千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198473_comment'></div>又辰州蛮人覃都、管骂等三十五栅团人，各纳土，输出贡，周围六百馀里，三千馀户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198473_comment'></div>及涪州夷人骆世华归顺中华地土，东西计六程，南北五程，情愿请税承输，未耕之地并乞入官，幅员一千一百馀里，至涪州一十三程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198473_comment'></div>汉夜郎地分，唐属黔中，措置建立州县城寨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198473_comment'></div>又上夷州首领任应举乞将所管夷州四县进纳入官，与置州县，输纳税赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198473_comment'></div>又下夷州首领任汉忠等，各愿将所管东西四程、南北五程见佃土地即请税承纳，馀尽献入官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198473_comment'></div>又南平军夷人木攀族首领赵泰等献土归化，见耕佃土地请税，作汉家百姓，其馀土地召人耕佃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198473_comment'></div>管界东西五程，南北六程，周匝十八程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198473_comment'></div>又播州夷人杨光言所管系唐朝所建地唐州，平生户一万馀家，乞献纳朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198473_comment'></div>又宽乐州、安砂州、谱州四州七源州县先次纳土归明，愿将所管州县纳税，永为王民，计二万人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1198473_comment'></div>一十六州三十三县五十馀峒，幅员之广又一万里，及赍到印记三十四颗，及具地图以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1198473_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年11月</a>　议靖和皇后谥。作品：靖和皇后谥议。<div id='poem_1198474' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198474' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198474?labeling=true' target='_blank'>靖和皇后谥议<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观二年十一月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1108年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198474")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198474_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198474'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198474'>臣尝读《诗》，《周南》言王者之风，而《关雎》以下则独称后妃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198474_comment'></div>至《大雅·思齐》之诗曰：「大姒嗣徽音，则百斯男」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198474_comment'></div>而序云：「文王之所以圣，盖感人之道神矣，孰得而议？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198474_comment'></div>所见者后妃之化而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198474_comment'></div>由后妃以观焉，则文王之圣可知矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198474_comment'></div>夫岂特文王然哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198474_comment'></div>舜之所以大，见于妫汭之嫔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198474_comment'></div>禹之所以神，见于涂山之翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198474_comment'></div>则古帝王之功，未有不始于内，而推之天下者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198474_comment'></div>洪惟我宋，圣神相授，真主嗣兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198474_comment'></div>天作之合，化先阃内，帝业以隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198474_comment'></div>盖方俪体宸极，则仪声茂实，既有以彰于一时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198474_comment'></div>及奄弃椒涂，则鸿名徽称，斯有以垂于万世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198474_comment'></div>是用稽于公卿大夫，以合天下公议，靡敢私也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198474_comment'></div>恭维大行皇后慈惠和徽，柔肃恭实，故尚书令秦正懿王之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198474_comment'></div>惟时正懿佐命艺祖，勋载旗常，庆流苗裔，是生淑哲，出应昌运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1198474_comment'></div>白龟见梦，朱蛇效祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1198474_comment'></div>载诞之夕，祥光满室；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1198474_comment'></div>来嫔之初，神僧授记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1198474_comment'></div>袆褕之尊，信有符矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1198474_comment'></div>故方养德闺门，则端庄静重，不妄言笑，身衣浣濯，靡有厌色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1198474_comment'></div>逮作配潜邸，正位坤仪，则功德之盛，超今绝古，粲然可纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1198474_comment'></div>若其祗奉九庙，则严恭以相祀事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1198474_comment'></div>致养慈德，则思媚以尽妇道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1198474_comment'></div>谓靡丽之饰伤俭也，故服御无珠玉之奉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1198474_comment'></div>谓私谒之风害德也，故外家无干请之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1198474_comment'></div>居母仪之贵，而能守礼执义，怀抑畏之小心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1198474_comment'></div>视嫔嫱之众，而能屈己达下，无嫉妒之诐行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1198474_comment'></div>然则后之德可谓至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1198474_comment'></div>属飞龙之御天，而有拱翼圣躬之勤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1198474_comment'></div>感占熊之应兆，而有诞育元嗣之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1198474_comment'></div>继生贵主，以启天支之蕃衍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1198474_comment'></div>章明阴教，以致阃内之雍熙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1198474_comment'></div>思贤才之为助，所以转佐圣德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1198474_comment'></div>择左右以诲子，所以协成义方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1198474_comment'></div>然则后之功可谓极矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1198474_comment'></div>矧乃鸡鸣而起，侍求衣也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1198474_comment'></div>齐明盛服，侍旰食也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1198474_comment'></div>言摭经史，化圣学也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1198474_comment'></div>挥毫洒落，法宸翰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1198474_comment'></div>族既蕃矣，则岁荐必以贤，而弗及于庸下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1198474_comment'></div>家既宠矣，则训弟必以学，而靡容于怠荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1198474_comment'></div>至于侍上宴閒，则裨政化而甚密；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1198474_comment'></div>为民祈福，则捐脂泽而不吝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1198474_comment'></div>此又徽美昭著，中外之所共仰者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1198474_comment'></div>方且崇清静之化，悟真乘之理，游心于恬淡，绝意于纷华，此又不玩于富贵，而超然独得者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1198474_comment'></div>历考在昔后妃之贤，如大行皇后，可谓鲜俪矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1198474_comment'></div>圣上感德大业，丕冒海宇，廓尔天造，渊然神化，鼓舞群生，莫窥其奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1198474_comment'></div>窃仰大行皇后之懿，则主上之所圣，可概见其万一已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1198474_comment'></div>夫以所示于行，则知存诸心者有不可量之善；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1198474_comment'></div>以所施于外，则知秘于内者有不胜述之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1198474_comment'></div>然则殚竹帛，罄金石，有不足以形容者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1198474_comment'></div>若乃汉魏以来，史氏所称身衣大练，装不务饰，无戏弄音乐之好者，犹且载美咏歌，流芳简册，曾何敢望大行皇后之德之美之髣髴哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1198474_comment'></div>圣上叹珩璜之弗御，悼窀穸之有期，睿情伤轸，典礼备举，乃诏有司扬德善，册丕称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1198474_comment'></div>皇哉铄乎，岂不慰明灵而协众愿哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1198474_comment'></div>谨按谥法曰：柔德教众曰靖，恭仁鲜言曰靖；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1198474_comment'></div>雍熙阃内曰和，闺门有礼曰和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1198474_comment'></div>恭维大行皇后，众德之所备，大名之所归，神人合契，罔不惟称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1198474_comment'></div>伏请谥曰靖和皇后。</div><div id='poem_sentence_58_1198474_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1109&endYear=1109')">1109年11月</a>　六月，徽宗亲近郭天信奏天文，密白日中有黑子，屡白不己，徽宗惧，蔡京引疾乞罢，致仕，为太师、守中太一宫使，诸恩并依现任宰相，仍朝朔望，提举编修哲宗实录，大朝会许立宰相班。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='3a4ac965071e4afca04c4b078a759ce7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3a4ac965071e4afca04c4b078a759ce7");'><span id='3a4ac965071e4afca04c4b078a759ce7_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=-100000&endYear=1125')">1125年</a>，79岁</div><div id='3a4ac965071e4afca04c4b078a759ce7' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年6月</a>　六月甲寅，复太子少师，依前楚国公致仕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年2月</a>　二月，蔡京复太师，赐第京师。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年2月</a>　苏州现天书木理字“大吉”作品：苏州现天书木理字贺表。<div id='poem_1198475' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198475' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198475?labeling=true' target='_blank'>苏州现天书木理字贺表</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和二年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198475")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198475_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198475'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198475'>伏睹知苏州盛章据百姓陈世隆斫开木一段，心有天书「大吉」二字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198475_comment'></div>寻同众官看验，字色正紫，与斧刃所斫适相合无间，向背窳垤，委是生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198475_comment'></div>其木理字盖即非伪造，奉表称贺以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1198475_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年3月</a>　三月，徽宗晏蔡京内苑太清楼。事后蔡京作《太清楼记》作品：太清楼侍宴记。<div id='poem_1198513' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198513' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198513?labeling=true' target='_blank'>太清楼侍宴记</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和二年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198513")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198513_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198513'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198513'>政和二年三月，皇帝制诏臣京宥过<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1198513", 1198513, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>眚愆</span>，复官就第，命四方馆使、荣州防御使臣童师敏赍诏召赴阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198513_comment'></div>臣京顿首辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198513_comment'></div>继被御札手诏，责以大义，惶怖上道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198513_comment'></div>于是饮至于郊，曲燕于垂拱殿，祓禊于西池，宠大恩隆，念无以称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198513_comment'></div>上曰：「朕考周宣王之诗：『吉甫燕喜，既多受祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198513_comment'></div>来归自镐，我行永久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198513_comment'></div>饮御诸友，炰鳖脍鲤』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198513_comment'></div>其可不如古者」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198513_comment'></div>诏以是月八日开后苑太清楼，命内客省使、保大军节度观察留后、带御器械臣谭稹，同知入内内侍省事臣杨戬，内客省使、保康军节度观察留后、带御器械臣贾祥，引进使、晋州管内观察使、勾当内东门司臣梁师成等伍人总领其事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198513_comment'></div>西上閤门使、忠州刺史、尚药局典御臣邓忠仁等一十三人掌典内谒者职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198513_comment'></div>有司请办具上，帝弗用，前三日幸太清相视其所，曰，于此设次，于此陈器皿，于此置尊罍，于此膳羞，于此乐舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198513_comment'></div>出内府酒尊宝器：琉璃、马瑙、水精、玻瓈、翡翠玉，曰：「以此加爵」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198513_comment'></div>致四方美味：螺、蛤、虾、鳜白、南海琼枝、东陵玉蕊，与海物惟错，曰：「以此加笾」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198513_comment'></div>颁御府宝带：宰相、亲王以玉，执政以通犀，馀花犀，曰：「以此实篚」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198513_comment'></div>教坊请具乐奏，上弗用，曰：「后庭女乐，肇自先帝肄业，大臣未之享，其陈于庭」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198513_comment'></div>上曰：「不可以燕乐废政」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1198513_comment'></div>是日视事垂拱殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1198513_comment'></div>退，召臣何执中、臣蔡京、臣郑绅、臣吴居厚、臣刘正夫、臣侯蒙、臣邓洵仁、臣郑居中、臣邓洵武、臣高俅、臣童贯崇政殿阅弓马所子弟武伎，引强如格，各命以官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1198513_comment'></div>遂赐坐，命宫人击鞠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1198513_comment'></div>臣何执中等辞请立侍，上曰坐，乃坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1198513_comment'></div>于是驰马举仗，翻手覆手，丸素如缀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1198513_comment'></div>又引满驰射，妙绝一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1198513_comment'></div>赐赉有差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1198513_comment'></div>乃由景福殿西序入苑门，就次以憩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1198513_comment'></div>诏臣蔡京曰：「此跬步至宣和，即昔言者所谓金柱玉户者也，厚诬宫禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1198513_comment'></div>其令子攸掖入观焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1198513_comment'></div>东入小花径，南度碧芦丛，又东入便门，至宣和殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1198513_comment'></div>止三楹，左右挟，中置图书笔砚，古鼎彝罍洗陈几案台榻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1198513_comment'></div>漆以黑，下宇纯朱，上栋饰绿，无文采。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1198513_comment'></div>东西庑侧各有殿，亦三楹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1198513_comment'></div>东曰琼兰，积石为山，峰峦间出，有泉出石窦，注于沼北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1198513_comment'></div>有御札「静」字榜梁间，以洗心涤虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1198513_comment'></div>西曰凝芳后曰积翠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1198513_comment'></div>南曰瑶林；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1198513_comment'></div>北洞曰玉宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1198513_comment'></div>石自壁隐出，崭岩峻立，幽花异木，扶疏茂密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1198513_comment'></div>后有沼曰环碧，两旁有亭曰临漪、华渚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1198513_comment'></div>沼次有山，殿曰云华，阁曰太宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1198513_comment'></div>左蹑道以登，中道有亭曰琳霄、垂云、骞凤、层峦，百尺高峻，俯视峭壁攒峰，如深山大壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1198513_comment'></div>次曰会春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1198513_comment'></div>阁下有殿曰玉华，玉华之侧有御书榜曰「三洞琼文之殿」，以奉高真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1198513_comment'></div>旁有种玉、缘云轩相峙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1198513_comment'></div>臣奏曰：「宣和殿阁亭沼，纵横不满百步，而修真观妙，发号施令，仁民爱物，好古博雅，玩芳缀华咸在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1198513_comment'></div>楹无金瑱，壁无珠珰，阶无玉砌，而沼池岩谷，溪涧原隰，太湖之石，泗滨之磬，澄竹山茶，崇兰香茝，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_43_1198513", 1198513, "Clauses/144/Comments/0")'>葩华</span>而纷郁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1198513_comment'></div>无犬马射猎畋游之奉，而有鸥、凫、雁、鹜、鸳鸯、鸂鶒，龟鱼驯驯，雀飞而上下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1198513_comment'></div>无筦弦丝竹、鱼龙曼衍之戏，而有松风竹韵，鹤唳莺啼，天地之籁，适耳而自鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1198513_comment'></div>其洁齐清灵，雅素若此，则言者不根，盖不足恤」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1198513_comment'></div>日午，谒者引执中以下入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1198513_comment'></div>女童乐四百，靴袍玉带，列排场下，肃然无敢謦咳者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1198513_comment'></div>宫人珠笼巾、玉束带，秉扇、拂、壶、巾、剑、钺，持香毬，拥御床以次立，亦无敢离行失次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1198513_comment'></div>皇子嘉王楷起居，升殿侧侍，进趋庄重，俨若成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1198513_comment'></div>臣执中等前贺曰：「皇子侍燕，宗社之庆」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1198513_comment'></div>乐作，节奏如仪，声和而绎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1198513_comment'></div>酒三行，上顾谓群臣曰：「承平无事，君臣同乐，宜略去苛礼，饮食起坐当自便无间」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1198513_comment'></div>执事者以宝器进，上量满酌以赐，命皇子宣劝，群臣惶恐饮釂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1198513_comment'></div>又以惠山泉、建溪毫盏烹新贡太平嘉瑞斗茶饮之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1198513_comment'></div>上曰：「日未晡，可命乐」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1198513_comment'></div>殿上笙、簧、琵琶、箜篌、方响、筝、箫登陛合奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1198513_comment'></div>宫娥妙舞，进御酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1198513_comment'></div>上执爵，命掌樽者注群臣酒曰：「可共饮此杯」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1198513_comment'></div>群臣俯伏谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1198513_comment'></div>上又曰：「可观」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1198513_comment'></div>群臣凭陛以观，又顿首谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1198513_comment'></div>又命宫娥抚琴擘阮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1198513_comment'></div>已而，群臣尽醉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1198513_comment'></div>臣窃考《鹿鸣》之什冠于《小雅》，而忠臣嘉宾得尽其心，既醉太平之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1198513_comment'></div>醉酒饱德，人有士君子之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1198513_comment'></div>在昔君臣施报之道，在于饮食燕乐之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1198513_comment'></div>太清自真祖开宴，以迄于今，饮食之设，供张之盛，乐奏之和，前此未有；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1198513_comment'></div>劝侑之恩，礼意之厚，相与无间之情，亦今昔所无，实君臣千载之遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1198513_comment'></div>而臣德輶智殚，曾不足仰报万分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1198513_comment'></div>昔仲甫徂齐，式遄其归；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1198513_comment'></div>而吉甫作诵，穆如清风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1198513_comment'></div>召虎受命，锡以圭瓒，虎拜稽首，对扬王休，作召公考，天子万寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1198513_comment'></div>然则上之施光，下之报宜厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1198513_comment'></div>而臣老矣，论报无所，切不自量，慕古人之□，谨稽首再拜，诵曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_75_1198513'>皇帝在御，政若稽古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1198513_comment'></div>昔周宣王，燕嘉吉甫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1198513_comment'></div>曰来汝京，实始予辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1198513_comment'></div>厥初有为，唱予和汝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1198513_comment'></div>式遄其归，远于吴楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1198513_comment'></div>劳还于庭，饮至于露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1198513_comment'></div>既又享之，其开禁御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1198513_comment'></div>有来帝车，相视其所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1198513_comment'></div>于此膳羞，于此乐舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1198513_comment'></div>海物惟错，于以加俎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1198513_comment'></div>何锡予之，实篚及筥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1198513_comment'></div>箫鼓锵锵，后庭委女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1198513_comment'></div>帝曰宣和，不远跬步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1198513_comment'></div>人昔有言，金柱玉户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1198513_comment'></div>帝命子攸，尔掖尔父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1198513_comment'></div>乃瞻庭除，乃历殿庑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1198513_comment'></div>绿饰上栋，漆朱下宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1198513_comment'></div>梁无则雕，槛不采组。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1198513_comment'></div>有石岩岩，有泉湑湑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1198513_comment'></div>体道清心，于此燕处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1198513_comment'></div>彼言厚诬，何恤何虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1198513_comment'></div>帝执帝爵，劝酬交举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1198513_comment'></div>毋相其仪，毋间笑语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1198513_comment'></div>有喜惟王，饮之俾饫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1198513_comment'></div>臣拜稽首，千载之遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1198513_comment'></div>君施臣报，式燕且誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1198513_comment'></div>臣拜稽首，明命是赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1198513_comment'></div>天子万年，受天之祜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_102_1198513_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1198513'><span class='label'>按：</span>《挥麈馀话》卷一，四部丛刊续编本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1198513_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年5月</a>　蔡京落致任，三日一至赴都堂议事。又掌起实权。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年5月</a>　乞免书门下省文字。作品：乞免书门下省文字奏。<div id='poem_1198476' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198476' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198476?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞免书门下省文字奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和二年五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198476")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198476_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198476'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198476'>门下省乃覆驳之地，臣乃兼而冒处，实有妨嫌，委紊官制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198476_comment'></div>望许臣免书门下省文字。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1198476_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年10月</a>　上玄圭。作品：上玄圭议。<div id='poem_1198477' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198477' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198477?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上玄圭议</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和二年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198477")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198477_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198477'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198477'>臣等伏蒙宣示古玄圭，其制两傍列十二山，长一尺二寸，上锐下方，上有云雨文，下无瑑饰，外黑内赤，中有小好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198477_comment'></div>温润光泽，制作奇古，大异常玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198477_comment'></div>臣等谨按圭之制尚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198477_comment'></div>自舜辑五瑞，修五玉，以班岳牧，说者谓圭在焉，然无见于经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198477_comment'></div>唯禹平水土，告厥成功，帝锡以玄圭，而圭之名于是始著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198477_comment'></div>玉为纯阳之精，有充实之美；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198477_comment'></div>土居中央，运四时，生万物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198477_comment'></div>故古之圣人以玉为圭，以重土为「圭」之文，有土有国者所当御，盖取诸地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198477_comment'></div>圣人统天地，御阴阳，妙万物，非特地道而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198477_comment'></div>天玄而地黄，天道致用于南，藏用于北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198477_comment'></div>坎为玄，天之正色也，此圭之所以用玄，盖取诸天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198477_comment'></div>舜殛鲧，命禹以平水土，则地功成矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198477_comment'></div>惟天为大，惟尧则之，则禹之归功于尧，非天不足以称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198477_comment'></div>今圭锐上，天也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198477_comment'></div>方下，地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198477_comment'></div>上有云行雨施之文，天成也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1198477_comment'></div>下静而无所瑑饰，地平也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1198477_comment'></div>天地之道，于是又备焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1198477_comment'></div>舜之所以命禹，禹之所以归尧，概见于此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1198477_comment'></div>尧舜无二道，二《典》之文互相备，《舜典》之所载，亦尧事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1198477_comment'></div>舜封十有二山，作十有二章，肇十有二牧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1198477_comment'></div>而是圭十有二寸，其两旁山亦如之，其制其数悉同，则为禹圭明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1198477_comment'></div>自尧舜而降，莫若三代，虽其损益不同，然体尧蹈舜，其道一揆，可得而稽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1198477_comment'></div>周王执镇圭，瑑饰以四镇之山，其中必有好，为受组之地，其长一尺二寸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1198477_comment'></div>周人放古，自为一代之制，惟王所执，以镇四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1198477_comment'></div>由是而观，则周之制盖本于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1198477_comment'></div>前乎尧有所未备，后乎尧无以复加，盖天下之大器也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1198477_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下缵禹之绪，与尧同功，天所复命，授以至宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1198477_comment'></div>而臣等亲逢尧舜，复考尧禹之制于千古之下，与万邦黎献舞手蹈足，不胜大庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1198477_comment'></div>谨稽首再拜，上议以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1198477_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1198477'><span class='label'>按：</span>《宋会要辑稿》瑞异一之二○。第三册第二○七四页又见《通鉴长编纪事本末》卷一二八。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1198477_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年10月</a>　请受玄圭。作品：请受玄圭表。<div id='poem_1198478' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198478' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198478?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请受玄圭表</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和二年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198478")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198478_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198478'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198478'>玄圭至宝，历世无传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198478_comment'></div>道之将兴，时若有待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198478_comment'></div>宜命攸司，以时展采。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198478_comment'></div>拂龟蠲吉，昭受大宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198478_comment'></div>以笃邦家之庆，以慰神民之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198478_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1198478_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年11月</a>　十一月，蔡京进封鲁国公。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1113&endYear=1113')">1113年闰4月1日</a>　题王希孟《千里江山图》作品：题王希孟千里江山图。<div id='poem_1198509' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198509' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198509?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题王希孟千里江山图<span class='inlineComment2'>（政和三年闰四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1113年闰4月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198509")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198509_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198509'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198509'>政和三年闰四月一日赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198509_comment'></div>希孟年十八岁，昔在画学为生徒，召入禁中文书库，数以画献，未甚工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198509_comment'></div>上知其性可教，遂诲谕之，亲授其法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198509_comment'></div>不踰半岁，乃以此图进，上嘉之，因以赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198509_comment'></div>臣京谓天下士在作之而已。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1198509_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1113&endYear=1113')">1113年11月</a>　加上神宗皇帝徽号。作品：加上神宗皇帝徽号册文。<div id='poem_1198422' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198422' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198422?labeling=true' target='_blank'>加上神宗皇帝徽号册文</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和三年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198422")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198422_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198422'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198422'>孝子嗣皇帝臣佶稽首再拜言：闻道不可名，其可名者非道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198422_comment'></div>然古我先王骏惠其先烈，罔敢遏佚，彊为之名，用祗命于上帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198422_comment'></div>其道隆德著，永世有辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198422_comment'></div>顾惟寡昧，奉承圣绪，夙夜基命宥密，肆其靖之，惟厥志是继，惟厥万事是述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198422_comment'></div>十有四年，道洽政治，民用丕变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198422_comment'></div>六府三事孔修，利用厚生惟和，鳏寡孤独有养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198422_comment'></div>什伍其丁壮，宾兴其贤能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198422_comment'></div>惟我神考睿知，稽古有为，海隅万里，罔不率俾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198422_comment'></div>西至积石，南至于牂牁、夜郎，富以备礼，和以广乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198422_comment'></div>亦惟我神考建法立制，克和厥中，盛德大业，光于四海，格于天地，无远弗届。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198422_comment'></div>大纲小纪，本数末度，有条而不紊，若卜筮罔不是孚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198422_comment'></div>亦惟我神考于古其训，以克用乂，永观厥成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198422_comment'></div>盖迄于今，天休滋至，地不爱宝，告成厥功，锡以元圭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198422_comment'></div>末予冲人，诞受厥命，靡敢安居，夙夜惟厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198422_comment'></div>迪惟前人光，施于我后嗣，稽谟自天，酌于师言，谨以法古，始立意度，增厥徽称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198422_comment'></div>今燎禋圜坛，大享祖庙，躬以玉册玉宝，加上曰体元显道法古立宪帝德王功英文烈武钦仁圣孝皇帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1198422_comment'></div>夫显名惟德，显德惟名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1198422_comment'></div>率时昭考，孝思惟则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1198422_comment'></div>洞洞属属，若在其上，爰伸命于皇帝，垂训来裔，以光我烈考于无极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1198422_comment'></div>谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1198422_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1113&endYear=1113')">1113年11月</a>　更定哲宗皇帝徽号。作品：更定哲宗皇帝徽号册文。<div id='poem_1198423' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198423' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198423?labeling=true' target='_blank'>更定哲宗皇帝徽号册文</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和三年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198423")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198423_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198423'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198423'>孝弟嗣皇帝臣佶谨再拜稽首言：臣闻昔者先王褒显其世德，名阶于功，言顺于事，传言万世，远而益彰，莫之能易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198423_comment'></div>顾德不类，嗣承先业，永惟大思，畀付之重，夙夜震惧，弗知攸报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198423_comment'></div>恭惟哲宗皇帝英武刚健，威德大业，著在典册，载于徽称，不可以加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198423_comment'></div>至于嗣政之始，恭默不言，蒙养圣功，沉潜刚克。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198423_comment'></div>爰自亲政，睿知浚发，南面而听，赫然昭彻，如日之升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198423_comment'></div>追念先烈，明发永怀，震悼诋诬，临朝出涕，除恶昭奸，靡有佚罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198423_comment'></div>外攘夷狄，以复境土；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198423_comment'></div>内修法度，是正纷更。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198423_comment'></div>上定郊丘之制，下复省耕敛征役之科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198423_comment'></div>天下靡然，喜于王化。<div class='inline'
