id='poem_sentence_9_1198423_comment'></div>复行熙宁、元丰之政，德意志虑，废而复兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198423_comment'></div>遵制扬功之美，继志述事之孝，孚于神明，冒于下土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198423_comment'></div>以迄于今，地平天成，海内乂安，万邦作孚，天锡之瑞，元圭自至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198423_comment'></div>考循初终，寔惟前人光施后裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198423_comment'></div>永惟盛美，罔敢居有，亦罔敢自功，参稽彝宪，佥协人言，德莫大于世前人之德，功莫先于昭先人之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198423_comment'></div>而往者所上徽称，未究斯意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1198423_comment'></div>名以宾实，实有馀而名不足，大惧不足以彰显丕烈，用伸命于上帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1198423_comment'></div>今燎禋圜坛，荐享太室，躬以玉册玉宝，改上曰宪元继道世德扬功钦文睿武齐圣昭孝皇帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1198423_comment'></div>恭惟在天之灵昭鉴于下，来格来宁，膺此名实，永孚于休无斁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1198423_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1113&endYear=1113')">1113年11月</a>　南郊天神降乞宣付史馆。作品：南郊天神降乞宣付史馆奏。<div id='poem_1198479' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198479' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198479?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南郊天神降乞宣付史馆奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和三年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198479")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198479_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198479'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198479'>天神降格，实为大庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198479_comment'></div>乞宣付史馆，播告天下，仍乞许臣等称庆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1198479_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1113&endYear=1113')">1113年11月</a>　冬祀飨太庙事乞宣付秘书省。作品：冬祀飨太庙事乞宣付秘书省奏。<div id='poem_1198480' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198480' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198480?labeling=true' target='_blank'>冬祀飨太庙事乞宣付秘书省奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和三年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198480")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198480_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198480'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198480'>臣等获以职事赞相大礼，伏睹陛下祗戒精专。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198480_comment'></div>前期斋沐，食不茹荤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198480_comment'></div>降辂于庙门之外，却伞去扇，步入斋宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198480_comment'></div>躬奉玉册架，上神宗徽号，泪沾裀褥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198480_comment'></div>逮荐飨入室毕，再诣神宗室，泪犹不止，执事之臣，莫不欷歔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198480_comment'></div>及奠玉圜坛，当御小次，乃端圭于小次之前，以俟亚献、终献行礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198480_comment'></div>臣等窃以陛下功成不居，归美先烈，礼行于庙，诚孝笃至，感动左右，祗虔祀事，不少憩息，遂致天人感格，应答如响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198480_comment'></div>臣等不胜欣庆，伏乞宣付秘书省，垂训万世。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1198480_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1113&endYear=1113')">1113年</a>　车驾祓褉西池。作品：车驾祓褉西池，拟应制。<span class='inlineComment2'>（祐陵癸巳岁蔡元长……王明清《揮塵録》揮麈後録餘話卷之一  176。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年10月5日</a>　题宋徽宗所画《鹰图》作品：题宋徽宗所画鹰图。<div id='poem_1198510' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198510' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198510?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题宋徽宗画御鹰图</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和四年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198510")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198510_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198510'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198510'>万物赋形，秉气于八方，随方受色，其形不同，其色亦异，莫能易也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198510_comment'></div>故鹏鴳不能移其色鸿鹄，鸾凤不能变其文于凫雁，乌黑鹭白，鸡丹雀黄，皆自然之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198510_comment'></div>鹰，西方之禽，其性鸷，其色苍，未闻有色白者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198510_comment'></div>皇帝陛下德动天地，仁及飞走，齐阴阳之化，同南北之气，无彼疆此界之隔，羽毛动植，易形变色，以应圣德之盛，为国嘉瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198510_comment'></div>臣昨得至后苑，见大鹰立架上，其色纯素，心甚异之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198510_comment'></div>伏蒙宣示《鹰图》，恍然若身再到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198510_comment'></div>雄姿劲翮，高鬐短颈，望之若浮云轻鸥，真所谓应诚而至者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198510_comment'></div>非特羽物效祥，神笔之妙，无以复加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198510_comment'></div>政和四年十月五日，太师、鲁国公臣蔡京谨题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1198510_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1198510'><span class='label'>按：</span>《辛丑消夏记》卷一，光绪三十一年刻本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1198510_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年3月</a>　乞率百僚表贺朱草。作品：乞率百僚表贺朱草奏。<div id='poem_1198481' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198481' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198481?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞率百僚表贺朱草奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和五年三月）</span><span class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198481_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198481'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198481'>伏蒙宣示南安军所生朱草，正类珊瑚，分枝共干，体柔色朱，实火德政平之应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198481_comment'></div>臣等不胜大庆，欲率百僚拜表称贺。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1198481_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年3月</a>　请奉安哲宗玉牒。作品：请奉安哲宗玉牒奏。<div id='poem_1198482' class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198482")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198482_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198482'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198482'>重修到哲宗皇帝玉牒，已具进纳，乞降付本院依神宗皇帝玉牒例，于宗正寺取旧玉牒并匣，别书写封进，请宝讫，择日迎引于玉牒殿奉安。</div><div id='poem_sentence_0_1198482_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年8月</a>　八月，建明堂，命蔡京为明堂使。作品：明堂制度奏。<div id='poem_1198483' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198483' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198483?labeling=true' target='_blank'>明堂制度奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和五年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198483")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198483_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198483'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198483'>夏后氏世室，堂脩十四步<span class='inlineComment2'>（方六尺为步。）</span>，广益七步半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198483_comment'></div>土室方四步，广益四尺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198483_comment'></div>木、火、金、水四室各方三步，广益三尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198483_comment'></div>商人重屋，堂脩七寻<span class='inlineComment2'>（八尺为寻。）</span>，崇三尺，四阿重屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198483_comment'></div>周人明堂，度九尺之筵，东西九筵，南北七筵，堂一筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198483_comment'></div>五室，凡室二筵，则五室各自方一丈八尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198483_comment'></div>三代之制，脩广不相袭，夏度以六尺之步，商度以八尺之寻，而周以九尺之筵，世每近，制每广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198483_comment'></div>今若以二筵为太室，方一丈八尺，则室之中设版位，礼器已不可容，理当增广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198483_comment'></div>今从周之制，以九尺之筵为度，太室脩四筵<span class='inlineComment2'>（三丈六尺。）</span>，广五筵<span class='inlineComment2'>（四丈五尺。）</span>，共为九筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198483_comment'></div>木、火、金、水四室各脩三筵，益四五<span class='inlineComment2'>（三丈一尺五寸。）</span>，广四筵<span class='inlineComment2'>（三丈六尺。）</span>，共七筵，益四尺五寸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198483_comment'></div>十二堂古无脩广之数，今亦度以九尺之筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198483_comment'></div>明堂、玄堂各脩四筵<span class='inlineComment2'>（三丈六尺。）</span>，广五筵<span class='inlineComment2'>（四丈五尺。）</span>，左右个各脩广四筵<span class='inlineComment2'>（三丈六尺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198483_comment'></div>青阳、总章各脩广四筵<span class='inlineComment2'>（三丈六尺。）</span>，左右个各脩四筵<span class='inlineComment2'>（三丈六尺。）</span>，广三筵，益四五<span class='inlineComment2'>（三丈一尺五寸。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198483_comment'></div>四阿各四筵<span class='inlineComment2'>（三丈六尺。）</span>，堂柱外基各一筵<span class='inlineComment2'>（九尺。）</span>，堂总脩十九筵<span class='inlineComment2'>（十七丈一尺。）</span>，广二十一筵。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1198483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1198483'><span class='label'>按：</span>十八丈九尺。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1198483_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_content_1198484'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198484'>臣等伏睹台州宁海县佃户何保所种禾内，有一稃三米，系是祥瑞。</div><div id='poem_sentence_0_1198484_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年11月</a>　开封府尹盛章奏本府狱空，道场有甘露降。作品：苏州狱空甘露降乞宣付史馆奏。<div id='poem_1198485' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198485' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198485?labeling=true' target='_blank'>苏州狱空甘露降乞宣付史馆奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和五年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198485")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198485_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198485'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198485'>伏睹开封府尹盛章奏，本府狱空，道场有甘露降于右狱柽柳窠上，夺目耀日，灿如珠玑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198485_comment'></div>京等奉表称贺，乞宣付史馆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1198485_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1116&endYear=1116')">1116年1月</a>　湖南常平刘钦奏芦荻冲平地得金，类灵芝祥云。作品：湖南连掘得金乞许拜表称贺奏。<div id='poem_1198486' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198486' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198486?labeling=true' target='_blank'>湖南连掘得金乞许拜表称贺奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和六年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198486")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198486_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198486'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198486'>伏睹湖南常平刘钦奏，去年六月十二日，地名芦荻冲，平地掘得金一块，类灵芝祥云，重九斤八两。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198486_comment'></div>同日淘得颗块金甚多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198486_comment'></div>及自七月二十日掘得碎金，后来至十二月十八日又据掘得金四百七两二钱，已差潭州司刑曹事王弼管押诣阙进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198486_comment'></div>乞与臣僚拜表称贺。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1198486_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1116&endYear=1116')">1116年1月</a>　元宵应制。作品：丙申岁闰元宵应制。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1116&endYear=1116')">1116年</a>　政和六年春师敏从驾过延福宴饮是日不果到府第以状申白京京以绝句答之。作品：答童师敏。<span class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198494' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198494?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞三省录黄等免系名衔奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和元年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198494")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198494_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198494'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198494'>昨蒙宽假，许朝五日，止省大事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198494_comment'></div>而臣年馀七十，礼当谢事，今三省录黄、画旨入进文字，与六曹奏钞、敕命行下，犹系臣名衔，著「不押」、「免书」字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198494_comment'></div>岂有身不任事，事非己出，系名其上，虚负天下之责，腼颜惭怍，罔知所措。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1198494_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1198494'><span ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年5月</a>　广武埽开直河大河安流乞宣付史馆。作品：广武埽开直河大河安流乞宣付史馆奏。<div id='poem_1198495' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198495' class='poemTitle id='poem_sentence_0_1198495_comment'></div>皆自陛下降香陈醮，致舒解广武危急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198495_comment'></div>臣不胜大庆，伏乞宣付史馆。</div><div class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198496' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198496?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蒙设普天大醮谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和元年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198496")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div id='poem_sentence_0_1198496'>臣伏蒙圣慈以臣夏秋疾病，特命于龙德太一宫设普天大醮，又亲制青词以见诚意，至日临幸醮筵，别制密词，亲手焚奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198496_comment'></div>仰惟异礼，今昔所无，殒首杀身，难以仰报。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1198496_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年9月</a>　提举三山河桥孟昌龄奏。作品：广武诸埽岸下生滩河行中道乞宣付史馆奏。<div id='poem_1198497' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198497' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198497?labeling=true' target='_blank'>广武诸埽岸下生滩河行中道乞宣付史馆奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和元年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198497")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198497_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198497'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198497'>伏睹提举三山河桥孟昌龄奏：奉御笔前去三山河措置西桥河道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198497_comment'></div>臣行历新堤诸埽，点检得南丞官荥毖所申，管下三十五埽，自河清及广武埽以下，至三山正东南丞地分以来，卧南行流，皆是向着埽分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198497_comment'></div>唯广武诸埽又居都城之上，腹背清汴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198497_comment'></div>比年以来，再轸圣虑，今岁涨水之后，诸埽岸下一例生滩，河行中道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198497_comment'></div>实由圣德昭格，上下神祇助顺，协济伟绩，诚非人力所致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198497_comment'></div>伏望宣付史馆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1198497_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年9月12日</a>　徽宗燕蔡京等大臣保和新殿，请见安妃，蔡京作《保和殿记》以献。作品：保和殿曲燕记。<div id='poem_1198514' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198514' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198514?labeling=true' target='_blank'>保和殿曲燕记</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和元年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198514")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198514_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198514'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198514'>宣和元年九月十二日，皇帝诏臣蔡京、臣王黼、臣燕王俣、臣越王偲、臣嘉王楷、臣童贯、臣嗣濮王仲忽、臣冯熙载、臣蔡攸燕保和殿，臣蔡鯈、臣蔡翛、臣蔡鞗、臣蔡行、臣蔡徽、臣蔡术侍，赐食文字库。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198514_comment'></div>于是由临华殿门入，侍班东曲水，朝于玉华殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198514_comment'></div>上步至西曲水，循𨢬醾架，至太宁阁，登层峦、林霄、骞凤、垂云亭，景物如前，林木蔽荫如胜，始至保和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198514_comment'></div>殿三楹，楹七十架，两挟阁，无䌽绘饰侈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198514_comment'></div>落成于八月，而高竹崇桧，已森然蓊郁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198514_comment'></div>中楹置御榻，东西二间列宝玩与古鼎彝器、玉芝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198514_comment'></div>左挟閤曰妙有，设古今儒书、史子楮墨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198514_comment'></div>右曰宣道，道家金匮玉笈之书，与神霄诸天隐文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198514_comment'></div>上御步前行至稽古阁，有宣王石鼓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198514_comment'></div>历邃古、尚古、鉴古、作古、传古、博古、秘古诸阁，藏祖宗训谟，与夏商周尊、彝、鼎、鬲、爵、斝、卣、敦、盘、盂，汉晋隋唐书画，多不知识，骇见，上亲指示，为言其概。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198514_comment'></div>因指阁内：「此藏卿表章字札无遗者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198514_comment'></div>命开匮，匮有朱隔，隔内置小匣，匣内覆以缯绮，得臣所书撰《淑妃刘氏制》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198514_comment'></div>臣进曰：「札恶文鄙，不谓袭藏如此，念无以称报」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198514_comment'></div>顿首谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198514_comment'></div>抵玉林轩，过宣和殿、列岫轩、天真阁、凝德殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198514_comment'></div>殿之东，崇岩峭壁高百尺，林壑茂密，倍于昔见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1198514_comment'></div>过翘翠、燕处诸阁，赐茶全真殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1198514_comment'></div>上亲御击注，汤出乳花盈面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1198514_comment'></div>臣等惶恐前曰：「陛下略君臣夷等，为臣下烹调，震悸惶怖，岂敢啜」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1198514_comment'></div>顿首拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1198514_comment'></div>上曰：「可少休」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1198514_comment'></div>乃出瑶林殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1198514_comment'></div>中使冯皓传旨留题殿壁，喻臣笔墨已具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1198514_comment'></div>乃题曰：「琼瑶错落密成林，桧竹交加午有阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1198514_comment'></div>恩许尘凡时纵步，不知身在五云深」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1198514_comment'></div>顷之就坐，女童乐作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1198514_comment'></div>坐间，赐荔子、黄橙、金柑，相间布列前后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1198514_comment'></div>命邓文诰剖橙分赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1198514_comment'></div>酒五行，再休许，至玉真轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1198514_comment'></div>轩在保和西南庑，即安妃妆閤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1198514_comment'></div>命使传旨曰：「雅燕酒酣添逸兴，玉真轩内看安妃」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1198514_comment'></div>诏臣赓补成篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1198514_comment'></div>臣即题曰：「保和新殿丽秋辉，诏许尘凡到绮闱」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1198514_comment'></div>方是时，人自谓得见妃矣，既而但画像挂西垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1198514_comment'></div>臣即以诗谢，奏曰：「玉真轩槛暖如春，只见丹青未有人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1198514_comment'></div>月里常娥终有恨，鉴中姑射未应真」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1198514_comment'></div>须臾，中使召臣至玉华閤，上手持诗曰：「因卿有诗，况姻家，自当见」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1198514_comment'></div>臣曰：「顷缘葭莩，已得拜望，故敢以诗请」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1198514_comment'></div>上大笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1198514_comment'></div>妃素妆，无珠玉饰，绰约若仙子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1198514_comment'></div>臣前进再拜叙谢，妃答拜，臣又拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1198514_comment'></div>妃命左右掖起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1198514_comment'></div>上手持大觥酌酒命妃曰：「可劝太师」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1198514_comment'></div>臣奏曰：「礼无不报，不审酬酢可否」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1198514_comment'></div>于是持瓶注酒，授使以进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1198514_comment'></div>再坐，彻女童，去羯鼓，御侍奏细乐，作《兰陵王》、《扬州散》古调。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1198514_comment'></div>酬劝交错，上顾群臣曰：「桂子三秋<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1198514", 1198514, "Clauses/135/Comments/2")'>七里香</span>」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1198514_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_47_1198514", 1198514, "Clauses/136/Comments/0")'>七里香</span>，桂子名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1198514_comment'></div>臣楷顷许对曰：「麦云九夏两歧秀」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1198514_comment'></div>臣攸曰：「鸡舌五年千岁枣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1198514_comment'></div>臣曰：「菊英九日万龄黄」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1198514_comment'></div>乃赓载歌曰：「君臣燕衎升平际，属句论文乐未央」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1198514_comment'></div>臣奏曰：「陛下乐与人同，不间高卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1198514_comment'></div>日且暮，久勤圣躬，不敢安」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1198514_comment'></div>上曰：「不醉无归」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1198514_comment'></div>更劝迭进，酒行无算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1198514_comment'></div>上忽忆绍圣春宴口号二句，问曰：「卿所作否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1198514_comment'></div>馀句云何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1198514_comment'></div>臣曰：「臣所进诗，岁久不记」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1198514_comment'></div>上曰：「朕是时以疾告假，哲宗召至宣和西閤，问所告假者，对曰：『臣有负薪之疾，不果预需云之燕』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1198514_comment'></div>哲宗曰：『蔡承旨有佳句曰：红蜡青烟寒食后，翠华黄屋太微间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1198514_comment'></div>不可不赴』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1198514_comment'></div>上曰：『臣敢不力疾遵奉』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1198514_comment'></div>是日待漏东华，哲宗已遣使询来否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1198514_comment'></div>语罢，命郝随持杯以劝，凡三酬，大醉，免谢扶出」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1198514_comment'></div>因沉吟曰：「记上下句有曰『集英班』者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1198514_comment'></div>继而曰：「牙牌晓奏集英班，日照云龙下九关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1198514_comment'></div>红蜡青烟寒食后，翠华黄屋太微间」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1198514_comment'></div>继又曰：「三天乐奏三春曲，万岁声连万岁山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1198514_comment'></div>欲识君臣同乐意，天威咫尺不违颜」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1198514_comment'></div>臣顿首谢曰：「臣操笔注思，于今二十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1198514_comment'></div>陛下语及，方省髣髴，然不记一字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1198514_comment'></div>陛下藩邸已知臣，盖非今日，岂胜荣幸」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1198514_comment'></div>再拜谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1198514_comment'></div>上轮指曰：「二十四年矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1198514_comment'></div>左右皆大惊，非圣人孰与夫此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1198514_comment'></div>臣又谢曰：「臣被知藩邸，受眷绍圣，两朝遭遇，臣驽下衰老，无毫发称报」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1198514_comment'></div>上曰：「屡见哲宗道卿但为章惇辈沮忌，不及用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1198514_comment'></div>朕时年八岁，垂髻侍侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1198514_comment'></div>一日，哲宗凝虑，默若有所思，问曰：『大臣以谓不当绍述，朕深疑之』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1198514_comment'></div>奏曰：『臣闻子绍父业，不当问人，何疑之有』？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1198514_comment'></div>哲宗骇曰：『是儿有大志如此』！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1198514_comment'></div>由是刘挚、吕大防相继斥逐，绍述自此始」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1198514_comment'></div>臣奏曰：「陛下曲燕御酒，乐欣交通，而追惟哲宗付托与绍述之始，孝友笃于诚心，非特臣之幸，社稷天下之幸」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1198514_comment'></div>因再拜贺，黼已下皆再拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1198514_comment'></div>上又曰：「尝记合食与卿否」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1198514_comment'></div>臣谢曰：「是时大礼禁严，厨饔不得入，贸食端邸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1198514_comment'></div>蒙陛下赐之，臣被遇自兹，终身不敢忘」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1198514_comment'></div>又曰：「崇政殿试，卿在西幕详定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1198514_comment'></div>时因入，持扇求书，得二诗，皆杜甫所作诗，曰：『户外昭容紫袖垂，双瞻御座引朝仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1198514_comment'></div>香飘合殿春风转，花覆千官淑景移』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1198514_comment'></div>又：『五夜漏声催晓箭，九重春色醉仙桃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1198514_comment'></div>旌旗日暖龙蛇动，宫殿风微燕雀高』」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1198514_comment'></div>臣曰：「崇宁初蒙宣谕，扇犹在」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1198514_comment'></div>上曰：「今尚在也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1198514_comment'></div>臣曰：「自古人臣遭遇，或以一能一技见知当时，名显后世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1198514_comment'></div>臣章句片言，二十年前已蒙收录，崇宁以来，被遇若此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1198514_comment'></div>君臣千载，盖非一日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1198514_comment'></div>君之施厚，臣之报丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1198514_comment'></div>臣无尺寸，孤负恩纪，但知感涕」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1198514_comment'></div>上曰：「卿可以安矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1198514_comment'></div>臣又奏曰：「乐奏缤纷，酒觞交错，方事燕饮，上及继述，下及故老，若朋友相与衔杯酒，接慇勤之欢，道旧论新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1198514_comment'></div>顾臣何足以当？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1198514_comment'></div>臣请序其事以示后世，知今日燕乐，非酒食而已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1198514_comment'></div>夜漏已<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_104_1198514", 1198514, "Clauses/306/Comments/0")'>二鼓</span>五筹，众前奏丐罢，始退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1198514_comment'></div>十三日，臣京序<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1198514_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_106_1198514'>至：原无，据右引补。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_106_1198514'></div><div id='poem_sentence_106_1198514_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1198514'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_105_1198514_0'>⑴ 《挥麈馀话》卷一。又见《九朝编年备要》卷二八，《通鉴长编纪事本末》卷一三一。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1198514_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年9月</a>　徽宗燕蔡京等大臣保和新殿，传旨留题殿壁。作品：留题保和殿壁。<div id='poem_514127' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_514127' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/514127?labeling=true' target='_blank'>留题保和殿壁</a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_514127")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_514127_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_514127'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_514127'>琼瑶错落密成林，桧竹交加午有阴。<div id='poem_sentence_0_514127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_514127'>恩许<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_514127", 514127, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>尘凡</span>时纵步，不知身在五云深。<div id='poem_sentence_1_514127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_514127'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_514127_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年9月</a>　至玉真轩传旨赓补成篇。作品：至玉真轩奉诏赓补。<div id='poem_514128' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_514128' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/514128?labeling=true' target='_blank'>至玉真轩奉诏赓补</a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_514128")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_514128_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_514128'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_514128'>保和新殿丽秋晖，诏许尘凡到绮闱。<div id='poem_sentence_0_514128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_514128'>雅燕酒酣添逸兴，玉真轩内看安妃。<div id='poem_sentence_1_514128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_514128'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_514128_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年9月</a>　既而见安妃像，即以诗谢奏。<div id='poem_514129' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_514129' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/514129?labeling=true' target='_blank'>见安妃像</a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_514129")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_514129_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_514129'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_514129'>玉真轩槛暖如春，只见丹青未有人。<div id='poem_sentence_0_514129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_514129'>月里常娥终有恨，鉴中姑射未应真<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_514129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_514129'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_514129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_514129'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_514129_0'>⑴ 《挥麈馀话》：宣和元年九月十二日，皇帝召蔡京等燕保和殿。传旨留题殿壁，京题琼瑶错落云云。至玉真轩，即安妃妆阁，命使传旨曰“雅燕酒酣添逸兴，玉真轩内看安妃”，诏京赓补成篇。京即题保和新殿云云。既而但见画像挂西垣，即以诗谢奏云云。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_514129_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年9月20日</a>　徽宗幸道德院观金芝，遂由景龙江泛舟至蔡京府第呜銮堂，命座赐酒，略用家人礼。徽宗曰：“今岁四幸呜銮矣!”蔡京作《呜銮记》以献。作品：皇帝幸鸣銮堂记。<div id='poem_1198515' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198515' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198515?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇帝幸鸣銮堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和元年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198515")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198515_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198515'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198515'>宣和元年九月，金芝生道德院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198515_comment'></div>二十日，皇帝自景龙江汎舟由天波溪至鸣銮堂，淑妃从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198515_comment'></div>臣京朝堂下，移班拜妃，内侍连呼曰「妃答拜」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198515_comment'></div>臣欲谢，内侍掖起，膝不得下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198515_comment'></div>上曰：「今岁四幸鸣銮矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198515_comment'></div>臣顿首曰：「昔人三顾，堂成已六幸，千载荣遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198515_comment'></div>鸣銮固卑陋，且家素窭无具，愿留少顷，使得伸尊奉意」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198515_comment'></div>上曰：「为卿从容」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198515_comment'></div>臣退西庑视庖膳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198515_comment'></div>上为举箸屡酬，欢笑如家人，六遣使持码碯大杯赐酒，遂御西阁，亲手调茶，分赐左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198515_comment'></div>妃亦酌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198515_comment'></div>遣使道由臣堂视卧内，嗟其弊恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198515_comment'></div>步至芝所，上立门屏侧，语臣曰：「不御袍带，不可相见，可去冠服」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198515_comment'></div>臣惶怖曰：「人臣安敢？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198515_comment'></div>罪当万死」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198515_comment'></div>上曰：「既为姻家，置君臣礼，当叙亲」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1198515_comment'></div>上亲以手持橄榄以赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1198515_comment'></div>时屏内御坐有嫔在侧，咫尺不敢望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1198515_comment'></div>众哗曰「妃也」，妃兴顾，遽起立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1198515_comment'></div>臣附童贯致礼，乃奏乞遣贯为妃寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1198515_comment'></div>上乃酌酒授贯，妃饮竟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1198515_comment'></div>上又酌为妃酬酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1198515_comment'></div>上调羹，妃剖橙、榴，折芭蕉，分馀甘，遣臣婢竟遗赐，曰：「主上每得四方美味新奇，必赐<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1198515", 1198515, "Clauses/64/Comments/0")'>师相</span>，无顷刻废忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1198515_comment'></div>谕<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1198515", 1198515, "Clauses/66/Comments/0")'>师相</span>，知无忘」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1198515_comment'></div>臣怀感叹谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1198515_comment'></div>上又赐酒，命贯酌，曰：「可与贯语」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1198515_comment'></div>贯为臣言：「君臣相与，古今无若者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1198515_comment'></div>臣呜咽嗟惜，因语：「身危，非主上几不保，如今日大理魏彦纯事是也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1198515_comment'></div>贯遽以闻，上骇曰：「御卿若此，小人犹敢尔？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1198515_comment'></div>昨日聂山对，请穷治彦纯，已觉其离间，故罢山尹事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1198515_comment'></div>朕岂以一语罪卿？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1198515_comment'></div>小人以细故罗织耳」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1198515_comment'></div>亟索纸，即屏上草诏释彦纯，山出知安州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1198515_comment'></div>上又命酒，使贯陪，遂醉，诸孙掖出。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1198515_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年</a>　请以季冬颁朔。作品：请以季冬颁朔奏。<div id='poem_1198498' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198498' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198498?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请以季冬颁朔奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198498")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198498_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198498'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198498'>周观治象于正月之始和，以十二月颁告朔于邦国，皆不在十月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198498_comment'></div>后世以十月者，祖秦朔故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198498_comment'></div>秦以十月为岁首，故《月令》以孟冬颁来岁之朔，今不当用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198498_comment'></div>请以季冬颁岁运于天下。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1198498_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年11月13日</a>　和御制己亥十一月十三日南郊祭天齐宫即事赐诗。作品：恭和御制己亥十一月十三日南郊祭天齐宫即事赐诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（王明清《揮塵録》揮麈後録餘話卷之一 174。）</span><div id='poem_514121' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_514121' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/514121?labeling=true' target='_blank'>恭和御制己亥十一月十三日南郊祭天斋宫即事赐诗<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年11月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_514121")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_514121_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_514121'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_514121'>雪晴至日日初南，帝举明禋祀事严。<div id='poem_sentence_0_514121_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_514121'>万瓦沟中寒色在，一轮空外晓光暹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_514121_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_514121'>云和龙轸开冰辙，风暖鸾旗拂冻檐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_514121_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_514121'>共喜天心扶圣德，珠玑更误宠恩沾。<div id='poem_sentence_3_514121_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_514121'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_514121_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_514122' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_514122' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/514122?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年11月13日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_514122_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_514122'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_514122'>展采齐明拱面南，浓云深入夜更严。<div id='poem_sentence_0_514122_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_514122'>风和不放琼英落，日暖高随玉漏暹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_514122_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_514122'>照地神光临午陛，鸣皋仙羽下重檐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_514122_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_514122'>五门回仗如天上，看举鸡竿雨露沾。<div id='poem_sentence_3_514122_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_514122'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_514122_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_514123' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_514123' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/514123?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年11月13日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_514123_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_514123'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_514123'>衮龙朱履午阶南，大辇鸾鸣羽卫严。<div id='poem_sentence_0_514123_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_514123'>玉轸乍回黄道稳，金乌初上白云暹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_514123_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_514123'>五门晓吹开旗尾，万骑花光入帽檐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_514123_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_514123'>已见神光昭感格，鹤书恩下万邦沾。<div id='poem_sentence_3_514123_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_514123'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_514123_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_514124' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_514124' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/514124?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年11月13日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_514124_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_514124'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_514124'>饮福初回八陛南，凝旒裒对百神严。<div id='poem_sentence_0_514124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_514124'>睍消尘入康衢润，神应光随北陆暹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_514124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_514124'>丹槛雉开中扇影，朱绳鹤下五门檐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_514124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_514124'>群生鼓舞明禋毕，却忆花飞舞袖沾。<div id='poem_sentence_3_514124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_514124'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_514124_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年6月</a>　乞致仕。作品：乞致仕劄子。<div id='poem_1198499' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198499' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198499?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞致仕劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和二年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198499")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198499_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198499'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198499'>臣以衰病，三上章陈乞致仕，伏蒙圣慈赐臣御笔，至比迹于周公，顾臣何人，敢当此礼？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198499_comment'></div>缘臣自被识拔，承辅轩陛，垂二十年，辨释谗谤，脱于患祸，天地父母之施，盖无以过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198499_comment'></div>又使间朝五日，疲老馀生，遂得休佚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198499_comment'></div>三省职事，许不省治，而恩礼频颁，有加无替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198499_comment'></div>联姻国戚，子尚王姬，赐予宠赉，略无虚日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198499_comment'></div>轻舟小辇，鸣銮七幸，婢妾仆皂，皆被恩荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198499_comment'></div>眷礼若此，安敢言去？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198499_comment'></div>偶缘比来体虚心弱，暑气所伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198499_comment'></div>七十谢事，礼不可踰，加以四年，已为贪冒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198499_comment'></div>况又疾病寖深，不能自已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198499_comment'></div>臣不敢再上表章，谨令男攸持此劄子请对投进。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1198499_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1198499'><span class='label'>按：</span>《宋会要辑稿》礼四七之一四（第二册第一四七七页）。又见同书礼四七之八（第二册第一四八一页）。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1198499_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年6月</a>　六月，蔡京致仕，仍朝朔望。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年12月</a>　宣和二年十二月癸巳，召宰执、亲王等曲宴于延福宫。作品：延福宮曲宴记。<div id='poem_1198516' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198516' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198516?labeling=true' target='_blank'>延福宫曲宴记</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和二年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198516")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198516_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198516'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198516'>宣和二年十二月癸巳，召宰执、亲王等曲宴于延福宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198516_comment'></div>特召学士承旨臣李邦彦、学士臣宇文粹中，与示异恩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198516_comment'></div>是日，初御睿谟殿，设席如外廷赐宴之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198516_comment'></div>然器用殽品瑰奇精致，非常宴比；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198516_comment'></div>仙韶执乐，和音曼声，合变争节，亦非教坊工人所能髣髴，上遣殿中监蔡行谕旨曰：「此中不同外廷，无弹奏之仪，但饮食自如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198516_comment'></div>食味、果实有馀者，自可携归」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198516_comment'></div>酒五行，以碧玉盏宣谕<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，少憩于殿门之东庑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198516_comment'></div>晚，召赴景龙门观灯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198516_comment'></div>玉华阁飞升，金碧绚耀，疑在云霄间，设衢樽钧乐于下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198516_comment'></div>都人熙熙，且醉且戏，继以歌诵，示天下与民同乐之恩，侈太平之盛事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198516_comment'></div>次诣穆清殿，后入崆峒洞天，过霓桥，至会宁殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198516_comment'></div>有八閤，东西对列，曰琴、棋、书、画、茶、丹、经、香。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198516_comment'></div>臣等熟视之，自崆峒入，至八閤，所陈之物，左右上下皆琉璃也，映彻焜煌，心目俱夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198516_comment'></div>閤前再坐，小案玉斝，珍异如海陆羞鼎，又与睿谟不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198516_comment'></div>酒三行甚速，起诣殿侧纵观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198516_comment'></div>上谓保和殿学士蔡翛曰：「引二翰苑子细看，一一说与」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1198516_comment'></div>谆谕再三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1198516_comment'></div>次诣成平殿，凤烛龙灯，灿然如画，奇伟万状，不可名言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1198516_comment'></div>上命近侍取茶具，亲手注汤<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1198516", 1198516, "Clauses/63/Comments/0")'>击拂</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1198516_comment'></div>少顷，白乳浮盏面，如疏星澹月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1198516_comment'></div>顾诸臣曰：「此自布茶」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1198516_comment'></div>饮毕，皆顿首谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1198516_comment'></div>既而命坐，酒行无算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1198516_comment'></div>复出宫人合曲，妙舞蹁跹，态有馀妍，凡目创见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1198516_comment'></div>上谕臣邦彦、臣粹中曰：「此尽是嫔御，自来翰林不曾与此集，自卿等始」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1198516_comment'></div>又曰：「《翰林志》谁修」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1198516_comment'></div>太宰王黼奏云：「承旨李邦彦」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1198516_comment'></div>上顾臣邦彦曰：「好！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1198516_comment'></div>《翰林志》可以尽载此事，此卿等荣遇」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1198516_comment'></div>臣邦彦谢不敏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1198516_comment'></div>琼瑶玉舟，宣劝非一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1198516_comment'></div>上每亲临视使釂，复顾臣某曰：「李承旨善饮」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1198516_comment'></div>仍数被特劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1198516_comment'></div>夜分而罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1198516_comment'></div>臣仰惟陛下加惠亲贤，共享太平，肆念词臣，许陪鼎席宗工之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1198516_comment'></div>周于待遇，略去常仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1198516_comment'></div>臣邦彦、粹中首膺异数，亲承玉音，俾编载荣遇，以侈北门之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1198516_comment'></div>盖陛下崇儒右文，表异鳌禁，用示眷瞩之意，诚千载幸会也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1198516_comment'></div>窃伏惟念，一介微臣，粤自布衣，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1198516", 1198516, "Clauses/114/Comments/0")'>叨膺</span>识擢，凡所蒙被，度越伦辈，曾微毫忽，以助山岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1198516_comment'></div>兹侍燕衎，咫尺威颜，独误睿奖，至官而不名，岂臣糜捐所能称塞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1198516_comment'></div>臣切观文武之盛，始于忧勤，而逸乐继之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1198516_comment'></div>《鹿鸣》之燕，群臣嘉宾得尽其心，故天保之报，永永无极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1198516_comment'></div>臣虽么陋，敢忘归美之义？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1198516_comment'></div>辄扬盛迹，备载于篇，使视草之臣知圣主曲宴内务，自臣等始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1198516_comment'></div>谨录进呈，伏取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1198516_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1198516'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_6_1198516_0'>⑴ 侍宴诸臣云：前此曲宴，早坐未尝宣劝，今出异数。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1198516_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a>　致仕闲居。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　蔡攸等出征。作品：送蔡攸征燕。<div inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>少休。<div id='poem_sentence_1_514119_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_514119'>目送旌旗如昨梦，心存关塞起新愁<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_514119_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_514119'>缁衣堂下清风满，早早归来醉一瓯<span class='inlineComment2'>（宋曾敏行《独醒杂志》卷五）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_514119_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_514119'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_514119_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_514119_0'>⑶ 《三朝北盟会编》作身非帏幄若为筹</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_514119_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年10月15日</a>　为道士杨大均祖考所书墓表。作品：道士杨大均祖考墓表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋文》系年于政和七年四月，当误。政和七年四月望为安葬之日，非京所书之日。）</span><div id='poem_1198523' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198523' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198523?labeling=true' target='_blank'>道士杨大均祖考墓表</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和七年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198523")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198523_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198523'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198523'>政和七年四月十五日，蔡州□宁万寿观道士杨大均葬祖考于汝阳县凤源乡北魏庄村之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198523_comment'></div>宣和四年十月望，太师、鲁国公蔡京书表其墓左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198523_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1198523_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年6月</a>　燕山大捷。作品：贺收复全燕表。<div id='poem_1198501' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198501' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198501?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺收复全燕表</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和五年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198501")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198501_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198501'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198501'>师由义动，往城于方；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198501_comment'></div>国以和来，不战而屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198501_comment'></div>举全燕之故地，吊介狄之遗民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198501_comment'></div>戴白垂髫，欢呼而解衽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198501_comment'></div>壶浆箪食，充塞而载涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198501_comment'></div>万国来同，一方底定，乾坤动色，庙社用光<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198501_comment'></div>惟北有邦，实冀之府，大禹所别，有虞尝巡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198501_comment'></div>粤我造邦之初，遂为与国之敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198501_comment'></div>始约兄弟，尊至祖孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198501_comment'></div>金缯缔交，使传洽至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198501_comment'></div>其强弗率，僭伪号者二百年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198501_comment'></div>有志未遑，更圣君之六七作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198501_comment'></div>惟昔神考，于时元丰，分将隶兵，联民讲武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198501_comment'></div>阅九军之师阵，建北面之黄旗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198501_comment'></div>无衅可乘，有训斯在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198501_comment'></div>皇帝陛下以重华而绍帝之事，以下武而继文之声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1198501_comment'></div>因其天亡之时，成是席卷之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1198501_comment'></div>臣顾惟稚长，久误眷知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1198501_comment'></div>诗礼之庭，屡趋而过；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1198501_comment'></div>军旅之事，盖未尝闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1198501_comment'></div>察之于谈笑杯酌之閒，付之以疆埸甲兵之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1198501_comment'></div>乘其万举万全之会，授之百发百中之机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1198501_comment'></div>是惟秉钺以专征，岂可因人而成事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1198501_comment'></div>山川草木，悉归舆地之图；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1198501_comment'></div>士女臣民，尽效职方之贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1198501_comment'></div>此盖皇帝陛下懋昭大德，遹骏先猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1198501_comment'></div>人斯效能，天实助顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1198501_comment'></div>扬励无前之伟绩，铺张不世之宏休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1198501_comment'></div>千载君臣，适遇风云之际；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1198501_comment'></div>一门父子，得为勋戚之家。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1198501_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1198501'><span class='label'>按：</span>《三朝北盟会编》卷一七，光绪三十四年许涵度刻本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1198501_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　燕山告功。作品：贺燕山告功表。<div id='poem_1198502' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198502' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年12月</a>　时河朔、青、齐间盗贼日炽，动数十万人，内外窘匮，莫能支吾。上意大不乐，上曰：“崇观间安至是哉!”上与中宫数有密议，然无人敢当其事。中宫赞上召故老大臣分付，上以为然，遂决意起京。上又恐京年高不能朝参，遂命其子以时入对，传道君臣之意。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年4月</a>　四月，蔡京引退致仕。<br />年份未详　政宣间，越州竹生花，徐州柏生花，太师蔡京作贺表。作品：贺越州竹生花表。<span -----title
河间
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='79782f7e7fdc4ca5ac1bb8f8f2617665_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("79782f7e7fdc4ca5ac1bb8f8f2617665");'><span id='79782f7e7fdc4ca5ac1bb8f8f2617665_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1089')">1087-1089年</a>，41-43岁</div><div id='79782f7e7fdc4ca5ac1bb8f8f2617665' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年12月</a>　知瀛州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年</a>　在瀛州任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1089')">1089年5月</a>　反变法派提出“王安石亲党”名单30人，“蔡确亲党”名单47人，列榜公布，不许在朝为官。蔡京兄弟在名单中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1089')">1089年6月</a>　本决定龙图阁待制、知瀛州蔡京为宝文阁直学士、知成都府。除命一出，谏官梁焘、范祖禹、吴安持、御史朱光庭等皆言其不可。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1089')">1089年6月25日</a>　诏京为江、淮、荆、浙等路发运使，罢宝文阁直学士、知成都府指挥。<br /></div>

-----title
定州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='357b31211e0c435ca6108028a82c08ff_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("357b31211e0c435ca6108028a82c08ff");'><span id='357b31211e0c435ca6108028a82c08ff_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>，55岁</div><div id='357b31211e0c435ca6108028a82c08ff' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年12月</a>　童贯以供奉官诣三吴访书画奇巧，留杭累月，京与游，不舍昼夜。凡所画屏幛、扇带之属，贯日以达禁中，且附语言论奏至帝所，由是帝属意京。又太学博士范致虚素与左街道录徐知常善，知常以符水出入元符后殿，致虚深结之，道其平日趣向，谓非相京不足以有为。已而宫妾、宦官合为一词誉京，遂擢致虚右正言，起京知定州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年12月22日</a>　苏州城南重修二庙。作品：重修南双庙記。<div id='poem_1198512' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1198512' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1198512?labeling=true' target='_blank'>重修南双庙记<span class='inlineComment2'>（建中靖国元年十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年12月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31303, "北宋", "蔡京", "poem_title_1198512")'>蔡京</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1198512_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1198512'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1198512'>今天子即位元年，爱重黎庶，慎简牧守，诏以左史吴公为直秘阁、知苏州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1198512_comment'></div>公至期岁，政化大洽，奸盗屏斥，牒讼疏简，民用康靖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1198512_comment'></div>公曰：「噫嘻！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1198512_comment'></div>先成民而后致力于神，古之善经也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1198512_comment'></div>今俗且治矣，其录境内神祠废坏者，以公帑所馀毕修之，使安定休止，无有祟厉，为吾民忧」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1198512_comment'></div>吏白：「城西南隅有旧庙二，荒陊当完。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1198512_comment'></div>按图经暨州县版祝所称，一为永昌武大王，一为福顺贤德王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1198512_comment'></div>而邦人由闾阎市井及学士大夫，自昔相传，皆以为伍子胥庙，岁时祭享甚盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1198512_comment'></div>杂然同辞，莫可夺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1198512_comment'></div>或言，故隋将陈果仁尝以阴兵助钱氏伐淮寇有功，钱氏崇报之，请于梁朝，封福顺王，又使诸郡皆为建庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1198512_comment'></div>则福顺之号为果仁无疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1198512_comment'></div>至永昌之称，杳邈不可稽考，不知为何时人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1198512_comment'></div>今邦人独以子胥之故，愿众私出力，以卒营缮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1198512_comment'></div>协谋齐虑，鸠工类材，填郛溢郭，奔走相属，惟恐其后，故月不更朔，而庙已告新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1198512_comment'></div>今或称号仍旧，殆恐无以妥子胥之灵，而失邦人所以完庙本意，敢以为请」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1198512_comment'></div>公曰：「然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1198512_comment'></div>昔吴濒海建国，恃水作险，内虞汎滥，外阙守御，蛙黾之与渚，而鱼鳖之与居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1198512_comment'></div>肇自子胥，相土味水，筑置城郭，实仓廪，治兵库，辟门二八，以象风卦，始能启塞有时，疏导无壅，除昏垫荡析之虞，而存抱关击柝之警。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1198512_comment'></div>更祀几百，历载踰千，其城域门号，至今因之而不变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1198512_comment'></div>是子胥尝能安吾民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1198512_comment'></div>不顾小义，卒雪大耻，勇于纳谏，以至殁身，二者皆人之所难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1198512_comment'></div>昔日之不死，盖以为吾父；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1198512_comment'></div>今日之死，盖以为吾君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1198512_comment'></div>由前足以教人之为孝，由后足以教人之为忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1198512_comment'></div>忠孝之迹，昭著前史，殊尤卓绝，震暴耳目，匹夫匹妇可以与知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1198512_comment'></div>及其久也，宜胥化焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1198512_comment'></div>故后汉太守麋豹按行属城，问风俗所尚，其功曹唐景曰：『处家无不孝之子，立朝无不忠之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1198512_comment'></div>傥非渐渍馀风，被服成俗，畴能臻此哉』！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1198512_comment'></div>是子胥尝能教吾民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1198512_comment'></div>既能安之，又能教之，由父传子，由子传孙，绵绵联联，以至今日，厥德茂矣，宜当血食此地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1198512_comment'></div>而庙貌不立于城阈，乃至斯民凭假它祠，以崇敬奉，此殆畴昔守职者之阙，吾敢不勉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1198512_comment'></div>《祭法》曰：『法施于民则祀之，以死勤事则祀之，以劳定国则祀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1198512_comment'></div>非此族也，不在祀典』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1198512_comment'></div>今福顺虽有功异代，事迹仅存，民弗敬慕，盖托子胥，获享不替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1198512_comment'></div>而武氏名字功德，阙然堙灭，无所考證；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1198512_comment'></div>使子胥不忘斯民，实鉴临之，则武亦安敢正位而飨也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1198512_comment'></div>礼固有以义起者，吾将请于天子，冀正英烈之号，以嘉庙额，而用丕承民志，殆或可乎」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1198512_comment'></div>武林元时敏曰：「好恶靡常，莫能自克，惟民为然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1198512_comment'></div>古之君子，因民所好之善而导之，反民所好之非而禁之，好恶得正，而其治成矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1198512_comment'></div>郑人欲祀伯有，子产从而封焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1198512_comment'></div>邺人欲祭河伯，西门豹从而禁焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1198512_comment'></div>二子岂异意哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1198512_comment'></div>顾民好恶有当否也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1198512_comment'></div>今吾民愿祀子胥甚勤，是知有功之不可忘，而忠孝之可劝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1198512_comment'></div>因而导之，使成于善，此所谓不严而治者，顾岂俗吏之所能为耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1198512_comment'></div>今公一举废事，而顺于民，安于神，又足为天下之劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1198512_comment'></div>三善备矣，不可不书也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1198512_comment'></div>于是乎书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1198512_comment'></div>建中靖国元年十二月二十二日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1198512_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1198512'><span class='label'>按：</span>绍定《吴郡志》卷一二，影印文渊阁四库全书本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1198512_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end
